5049 void MacroAssembler::reinit_heapbase() {
5050   if (UseCompressedOops || UseCompressedClassPointers) {
5051     if (Universe::heap() != NULL) {
5052       if (CompressedOops::base() == NULL) {
5053         MacroAssembler::xorptr(r12_heapbase, r12_heapbase);
5054       } else {
5055         mov64(r12_heapbase, (int64_t)CompressedOops::ptrs_base());
5056       }
5057     } else {
5058       movptr(r12_heapbase, ExternalAddress((address)CompressedOops::ptrs_base_addr()));
5059     }
5060   }
5061 }
5062 
5063 #endif // _LP64
5064 
5065 // C2 compiled method's prolog code.
5066 void MacroAssembler::verified_entry(Compile* C, int sp_inc) {
5067   int framesize = C->output()->frame_size_in_bytes();
5068   int bangsize = C->output()->bang_size_in_bytes();
5069   bool fp_mode_24b = false;
5070   int stack_bang_size = C->output()->need_stack_bang(bangsize) ? bangsize : 0;
5071 
5072   // WARNING: Initial instruction MUST be 5 bytes or longer so that
5073   // NativeJump::patch_verified_entry will be able to patch out the entry
5074   // code safely. The push to verify stack depth is ok at 5 bytes,
5075   // the frame allocation can be either 3 or 6 bytes. So if we don't do
5076   // stack bang then we must use the 6 byte frame allocation even if
5077   // we have no frame. :-(
5078   assert(stack_bang_size >= framesize || stack_bang_size <= 0, "stack bang size incorrect");
5079 
5080   assert((framesize & (StackAlignmentInBytes-1)) == 0, "frame size not aligned");
5081   // Remove word for return addr
5082   framesize -= wordSize;
5083   stack_bang_size -= wordSize;
5084 
5085   // Calls to C2R adapters often do not accept exceptional returns.
5086   // We require that their callers must bang for them.  But be careful, because
5087   // some VM calls (such as call site linkage) can use several kilobytes of
5088   // stack.  But the stack safety zone should account for that.
5089   // See bugs 4446381, 4468289, 4497237.
5090   if (stack_bang_size > 0) {
5091     generate_stack_overflow_check(stack_bang_size);
5092 
5093     // We always push rbp, so that on return to interpreter rbp, will be
5094     // restored correctly and we can correct the stack.
5095     push(rbp);
5096     // Save caller's stack pointer into RBP if the frame pointer is preserved.
5097     if (PreserveFramePointer) {
5098       mov(rbp, rsp);
5099     }
5100     // Remove word for ebp
5101     framesize -= wordSize;
5102 
5103     // Create frame
5104     if (framesize) {
5105       subptr(rsp, framesize);
5106     }
5107   } else {
5108     // Create frame (force generation of a 4 byte immediate value)
5109     subptr_imm32(rsp, framesize);
5110 
5111     // Save RBP register now.
5112     framesize -= wordSize;
5113     movptr(Address(rsp, framesize), rbp);
5114     // Save caller's stack pointer into RBP if the frame pointer is preserved.
5115     if (PreserveFramePointer) {
5116       movptr(rbp, rsp);
5117       if (framesize > 0) {
5118         addptr(rbp, framesize);
5119       }
5120     }
5121   }
5122 
5123   if (C->needs_stack_repair()) {
5124     // Save stack increment (also account for fixed framesize and rbp)
5125     assert((sp_inc & (StackAlignmentInBytes-1)) == 0, "stack increment not aligned");
5126     movptr(Address(rsp, C->output()->sp_inc_offset()), sp_inc + framesize + wordSize);
5127   }
5128 
5129   if (VerifyStackAtCalls) { // Majik cookie to verify stack depth
5130     framesize -= wordSize;
5131     movptr(Address(rsp, framesize), (int32_t)0xbadb100d);
5132   }
5133 
5134 #ifndef _LP64
5135   // If method sets FPU control word do it now
5136   if (fp_mode_24b) {
5137     fldcw(ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::addr_fpu_cntrl_wrd_24()));
5138   }
5139   if (UseSSE >= 2 && VerifyFPU) {
5140     verify_FPU(0, "FPU stack must be clean on entry");
5141   }
5142 #endif
5143 
5144 #ifdef ASSERT
5145   if (VerifyStackAtCalls) {
5146     Label L;
5147     push(rax);
5148     mov(rax, rsp);
5149     andptr(rax, StackAlignmentInBytes-1);
5150     cmpptr(rax, StackAlignmentInBytes-wordSize);
5151     pop(rax);
5152     jcc(Assembler::equal, L);
5153     STOP("Stack is not properly aligned!");
5154     bind(L);
5155   }
5156 #endif
5157 }
5158 
5159 // clear memory of size 'cnt' qwords, starting at 'base' using XMM/YMM registers
5160 void MacroAssembler::xmm_clear_mem(Register base, Register cnt, Register val, XMMRegister xtmp) {
5161   // cnt - number of qwords (8-byte words).
5162   // base - start address, qword aligned.
5163   Label L_zero_64_bytes, L_loop, L_sloop, L_tail, L_end;
5164   movdq(xtmp, val);
5165   if (UseAVX >= 2) {
5166     punpcklqdq(xtmp, xtmp);
5167     vinserti128_high(xtmp, xtmp);
5168   } else {
5169     punpcklqdq(xtmp, xtmp);
5170   }
5171   jmp(L_zero_64_bytes);
5172 
5173   BIND(L_loop);
5174   if (UseAVX >= 2) {
5175     vmovdqu(Address(base,  0), xtmp);
5176     vmovdqu(Address(base, 32), xtmp);
5177   } else {
5178     movdqu(Address(base,  0), xtmp);
5179     movdqu(Address(base, 16), xtmp);
5180     movdqu(Address(base, 32), xtmp);
5181     movdqu(Address(base, 48), xtmp);
5182   }
5183   addptr(base, 64);
5184 
5185   BIND(L_zero_64_bytes);
5186   subptr(cnt, 8);
5187   jccb(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_loop);
5188   addptr(cnt, 4);
5189   jccb(Assembler::less, L_tail);
5190   // Copy trailing 32 bytes
5191   if (UseAVX >= 2) {
5192     vmovdqu(Address(base, 0), xtmp);
5193   } else {
5194     movdqu(Address(base,  0), xtmp);
5195     movdqu(Address(base, 16), xtmp);
5196   }
5197   addptr(base, 32);
5198   subptr(cnt, 4);
5199 
5200   BIND(L_tail);
5201   addptr(cnt, 4);
5202   jccb(Assembler::lessEqual, L_end);
5203   decrement(cnt);
5204 
5205   BIND(L_sloop);
5206   movq(Address(base, 0), xtmp);
5207   addptr(base, 8);
5208   decrement(cnt);
5209   jccb(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_sloop);
5210   BIND(L_end);
5211 }
5212 
5213 int MacroAssembler::store_value_type_fields_to_buf(ciValueKlass* vk, bool from_interpreter) {
5214   // A value type might be returned. If fields are in registers we
5215   // need to allocate a value type instance and initialize it with
5216   // the value of the fields.
5217   Label skip;
5218   // We only need a new buffered value if a new one is not returned
5219   testptr(rax, 1);
5220   jcc(Assembler::zero, skip);
5221   int call_offset = -1;
5222 
5223 #ifdef _LP64
5224   Label slow_case;
5225 
5226   // Try to allocate a new buffered value (from the heap)
5227   if (UseTLAB) {
5228     // FIXME -- for smaller code, the inline allocation (and the slow case) should be moved inside the pack handler.
5229     if (vk != NULL) {
5230       // Called from C1, where the return type is statically known.
5231       movptr(rbx, (intptr_t)vk->get_ValueKlass());
5232       jint lh = vk->layout_helper();
5233       assert(lh != Klass::_lh_neutral_value, "inline class in return type must have been resolved");
5234       movl(r14, lh);
5235     } else {
5236       // Call from interpreter. RAX contains ((the ValueKlass* of the return type) | 0x01)
5237       mov(rbx, rax);
5238       andptr(rbx, -2);
5239       movl(r14, Address(rbx, Klass::layout_helper_offset()));
5240     }
5241 
5242     movptr(r13, Address(r15_thread, in_bytes(JavaThread::tlab_top_offset())));
5243     lea(r14, Address(r13, r14, Address::times_1));
5244     cmpptr(r14, Address(r15_thread, in_bytes(JavaThread::tlab_end_offset())));
5245     jcc(Assembler::above, slow_case);
5246     movptr(Address(r15_thread, in_bytes(JavaThread::tlab_top_offset())), r14);
5247     movptr(Address(r13, oopDesc::mark_offset_in_bytes()), (intptr_t)markWord::always_locked_prototype().value());
5248 
5249     xorl(rax, rax); // use zero reg to clear memory (shorter code)
5250     store_klass_gap(r13, rax);  // zero klass gap for compressed oops
5251 
5252     if (vk == NULL) {
5253       // store_klass corrupts rbx, so save it in rax for later use (interpreter case only).
5254       mov(rax, rbx);
5255     }
5256     store_klass(r13, rbx);  // klass
5257 
5258     // We have our new buffered value, initialize its fields with a
5259     // value class specific handler
5260     if (vk != NULL) {
5261       // FIXME -- do the packing in-line to avoid the runtime call
5262       mov(rax, r13);
5263       call(RuntimeAddress(vk->pack_handler())); // no need for call info as this will not safepoint.
5264     } else {
5265       movptr(rbx, Address(rax, InstanceKlass::adr_valueklass_fixed_block_offset()));
5266       movptr(rbx, Address(rbx, ValueKlass::pack_handler_offset()));
5267       mov(rax, r13);
5268       call(rbx);
5269     }
5270     jmp(skip);
5271   }
5272 
5273   bind(slow_case);
5274   // We failed to allocate a new value, fall back to a runtime
5275   // call. Some oop field may be live in some registers but we can't
5276   // tell. That runtime call will take care of preserving them
5277   // across a GC if there's one.
5278 #endif
5279 
5280   if (from_interpreter) {
5281     super_call_VM_leaf(StubRoutines::store_value_type_fields_to_buf());
5282   } else {
5283     call(RuntimeAddress(StubRoutines::store_value_type_fields_to_buf()));
5284     call_offset = offset();
5285   }
5286 
5287   bind(skip);
5288   return call_offset;
5289 }
5290 
5291 
5292 // Move a value between registers/stack slots and update the reg_state
5293 bool MacroAssembler::move_helper(VMReg from, VMReg to, BasicType bt, RegState reg_state[], int ret_off, int extra_stack_offset) {
5294   if (reg_state[to->value()] == reg_written) {
5295     return true; // Already written
5296   }
5297   if (from != to && bt != T_VOID) {
5298     if (reg_state[to->value()] == reg_readonly) {
5299       return false; // Not yet writable
5300     }
5301     if (from->is_reg()) {
5302       if (to->is_reg()) {
5303         if (from->is_XMMRegister()) {
5304           if (bt == T_DOUBLE) {
5305             movdbl(to->as_XMMRegister(), from->as_XMMRegister());
5306           } else {
5307             assert(bt == T_FLOAT, "must be float");
5308             movflt(to->as_XMMRegister(), from->as_XMMRegister());
5309           }
5310         } else {
5311           movq(to->as_Register(), from->as_Register());
5312         }
5313       } else {
5314         int st_off = to->reg2stack() * VMRegImpl::stack_slot_size + extra_stack_offset;
5315         assert(st_off != ret_off, "overwriting return address at %d", st_off);
5316         Address to_addr = Address(rsp, st_off);
5317         if (from->is_XMMRegister()) {
5318           if (bt == T_DOUBLE) {
5319             movdbl(to_addr, from->as_XMMRegister());
5320           } else {
5321             assert(bt == T_FLOAT, "must be float");
5322             movflt(to_addr, from->as_XMMRegister());
5323           }
5324         } else {
5325           movq(to_addr, from->as_Register());
5326         }
5327       }
5328     } else {
5329       Address from_addr = Address(rsp, from->reg2stack() * VMRegImpl::stack_slot_size + extra_stack_offset);
5330       if (to->is_reg()) {
5331         if (to->is_XMMRegister()) {
5332           if (bt == T_DOUBLE) {
5333             movdbl(to->as_XMMRegister(), from_addr);
5334           } else {
5335             assert(bt == T_FLOAT, "must be float");
5336             movflt(to->as_XMMRegister(), from_addr);
5337           }
5338         } else {
5339           movq(to->as_Register(), from_addr);
5340         }
5341       } else {
5342         int st_off = to->reg2stack() * VMRegImpl::stack_slot_size + extra_stack_offset;
5343         assert(st_off != ret_off, "overwriting return address at %d", st_off);
5344         movq(r13, from_addr);
5345         movq(Address(rsp, st_off), r13);
5346       }
5347     }
5348   }
5349   // Update register states
5350   reg_state[from->value()] = reg_writable;
5351   reg_state[to->value()] = reg_written;
5352   return true;
5353 }
5354 
5355 // Read all fields from a value type oop and store the values in registers/stack slots
5356 bool MacroAssembler::unpack_value_helper(const GrowableArray<SigEntry>* sig, int& sig_index, VMReg from, VMRegPair* regs_to,
5357                                          int& to_index, RegState reg_state[], int ret_off, int extra_stack_offset) {
5358   Register fromReg = from->is_reg() ? from->as_Register() : noreg;
5359   assert(sig->at(sig_index)._bt == T_VOID, "should be at end delimiter");
5360 
5361   int vt = 1;
5362   bool done = true;
5363   bool mark_done = true;
5364   do {
5365     sig_index--;
5366     BasicType bt = sig->at(sig_index)._bt;
5367     if (bt == T_VALUETYPE) {
5368       vt--;
5369     } else if (bt == T_VOID &&
5370                sig->at(sig_index-1)._bt != T_LONG &&
5371                sig->at(sig_index-1)._bt != T_DOUBLE) {
5372       vt++;
5373     } else if (SigEntry::is_reserved_entry(sig, sig_index)) {
5374       to_index--; // Ignore this
5375     } else {
5376       assert(to_index >= 0, "invalid to_index");
5377       VMRegPair pair_to = regs_to[to_index--];
5378       VMReg to = pair_to.first();
5379 
5380       if (bt == T_VOID) continue;
5381 
5382       int idx = (int)to->value();
5383       if (reg_state[idx] == reg_readonly) {
5384          if (idx != from->value()) {
5385            mark_done = false;
5386          }
5387          done = false;
5388          continue;
5389       } else if (reg_state[idx] == reg_written) {
5390         continue;
5391       } else {
5392         assert(reg_state[idx] == reg_writable, "must be writable");
5393         reg_state[idx] = reg_written;
5394        }
5395 
5396       if (fromReg == noreg) {
5397         int st_off = from->reg2stack() * VMRegImpl::stack_slot_size + extra_stack_offset;
5398         movq(r10, Address(rsp, st_off));
5399         fromReg = r10;
5400       }
5401 
5402       int off = sig->at(sig_index)._offset;
5403       assert(off > 0, "offset in object should be positive");
5404       bool is_oop = (bt == T_OBJECT || bt == T_ARRAY);
5405 
5406       Address fromAddr = Address(fromReg, off);
5407       bool is_signed = (bt != T_CHAR) && (bt != T_BOOLEAN);
5408       if (!to->is_XMMRegister()) {
5409         Register dst = to->is_stack() ? r13 : to->as_Register();
5410         if (is_oop) {
5411           load_heap_oop(dst, fromAddr);
5412         } else {
5413           load_sized_value(dst, fromAddr, type2aelembytes(bt), is_signed);
5414         }
5415         if (to->is_stack()) {
5416           int st_off = to->reg2stack() * VMRegImpl::stack_slot_size + extra_stack_offset;
5417           assert(st_off != ret_off, "overwriting return address at %d", st_off);
5418           movq(Address(rsp, st_off), dst);
5419         }
5420       } else {
5421         if (bt == T_DOUBLE) {
5422           movdbl(to->as_XMMRegister(), fromAddr);
5423         } else {
5424           assert(bt == T_FLOAT, "must be float");
5425           movflt(to->as_XMMRegister(), fromAddr);
5426         }
5427       }
5428     }
5429   } while (vt != 0);
5430   if (mark_done && reg_state[from->value()] != reg_written) {
5431     // This is okay because no one else will write to that slot
5432     reg_state[from->value()] = reg_writable;
5433   }
5434   return done;
5435 }
5436 
5437 // Pack fields back into a value type oop
5438 bool MacroAssembler::pack_value_helper(const GrowableArray<SigEntry>* sig, int& sig_index, int vtarg_index,
5439                                        VMReg to, VMRegPair* regs_from, int regs_from_count, int& from_index, RegState reg_state[],
5440                                        int ret_off, int extra_stack_offset) {
5441   assert(sig->at(sig_index)._bt == T_VALUETYPE, "should be at end delimiter");
5442   assert(to->is_valid(), "must be");
5443 
5444   if (reg_state[to->value()] == reg_written) {
5445     skip_unpacked_fields(sig, sig_index, regs_from, regs_from_count, from_index);
5446     return true; // Already written
5447   }
5448 
5449   Register val_array = rax;
5450   Register val_obj_tmp = r11;
5451   Register from_reg_tmp = r14; // Be careful with r14 because it's used for spilling
5452   Register tmp1 = r10;
5453   Register tmp2 = r13;
5454   Register tmp3 = rbx;
5455   Register val_obj = to->is_stack() ? val_obj_tmp : to->as_Register();
5456 
5457   if (reg_state[to->value()] == reg_readonly) {
5458     if (!is_reg_in_unpacked_fields(sig, sig_index, to, regs_from, regs_from_count, from_index)) {
5459       skip_unpacked_fields(sig, sig_index, regs_from, regs_from_count, from_index);
5460       return false; // Not yet writable
5461     }
5462     val_obj = val_obj_tmp;
5463   }
5464 
5465   int index = arrayOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes(T_OBJECT) + vtarg_index * type2aelembytes(T_VALUETYPE);
5466   load_heap_oop(val_obj, Address(val_array, index));
5467 
5468   ScalarizedValueArgsStream stream(sig, sig_index, regs_from, regs_from_count, from_index);
5469   VMRegPair from_pair;
5470   BasicType bt;
5471   while (stream.next(from_pair, bt)) {
5472     int off = sig->at(stream.sig_cc_index())._offset;
5473     assert(off > 0, "offset in object should be positive");
5474     bool is_oop = (bt == T_OBJECT || bt == T_ARRAY);
5475     size_t size_in_bytes = is_java_primitive(bt) ? type2aelembytes(bt) : wordSize;
5476 
5477     VMReg from_r1 = from_pair.first();
5478     VMReg from_r2 = from_pair.second();
5479 
5480     // Pack the scalarized field into the value object.
5481     Address dst(val_obj, off);
5482     if (!from_r1->is_XMMRegister()) {
5483       Register from_reg;
5484       if (from_r1->is_stack()) {
5485         from_reg = from_reg_tmp;
5486         int ld_off = from_r1->reg2stack() * VMRegImpl::stack_slot_size + extra_stack_offset;
5487         load_sized_value(from_reg, Address(rsp, ld_off), size_in_bytes, /* is_signed */ false);
5488       } else {
5489         from_reg = from_r1->as_Register();
5490       }
5491       assert_different_registers(dst.base(), from_reg, tmp1, tmp2, tmp3, val_array);
5492       if (is_oop) {
5493         store_heap_oop(dst, from_reg, tmp1, tmp2, tmp3, IN_HEAP | ACCESS_WRITE | IS_DEST_UNINITIALIZED);
5494       } else {
5495         store_sized_value(dst, from_reg, size_in_bytes);
5496       }
5497     } else {
5498       if (from_r2->is_valid()) {
5499         movdbl(dst, from_r1->as_XMMRegister());
5500       } else {
5501         movflt(dst, from_r1->as_XMMRegister());
5502       }
5503     }
5504     reg_state[from_r1->value()] = reg_writable;
5505   }
5506   sig_index = stream.sig_cc_index();
5507   from_index = stream.regs_cc_index();
5508 
5509   assert(reg_state[to->value()] == reg_writable, "must have already been read");
5510   bool success = move_helper(val_obj->as_VMReg(), to, T_OBJECT, reg_state, ret_off, extra_stack_offset);
5511   assert(success, "to register must be writeable");
5512 
5513   return true;
5514 }
5515 
5516 // Unpack all value type arguments passed as oops
5517 void MacroAssembler::unpack_value_args(Compile* C, bool receiver_only) {
5518   int sp_inc = unpack_value_args_common(C, receiver_only);
5519   // Emit code for verified entry and save increment for stack repair on return
5520   verified_entry(C, sp_inc);
5521 }
5522 
5523 void MacroAssembler::shuffle_value_args(bool is_packing, bool receiver_only, int extra_stack_offset,
5524                                         BasicType* sig_bt, const GrowableArray<SigEntry>* sig_cc,
5525                                         int args_passed, int args_on_stack, VMRegPair* regs,
5526                                         int args_passed_to, int args_on_stack_to, VMRegPair* regs_to, int sp_inc) {
5527   // Check if we need to extend the stack for packing/unpacking
5528   if (sp_inc > 0 && !is_packing) {
5529     // Save the return address, adjust the stack (make sure it is properly
5530     // 16-byte aligned) and copy the return address to the new top of the stack.
5531     // (Note: C1 does this in C1_MacroAssembler::scalarized_entry).
5532     pop(r13);
5533     subptr(rsp, sp_inc);
5534     push(r13);
5535   }
5536 
5537   int ret_off; // make sure we don't overwrite the return address
5538   if (is_packing) {
5539     // For C1 code, the VVEP doesn't have reserved slots, so we store the returned address at
5540     // rsp[0] during shuffling.
5541     ret_off = 0;
5542   } else {
5543     // C2 code ensures that sp_inc is a reserved slot.
5544     ret_off = sp_inc;
5545   }
5546 
5547   shuffle_value_args_common(is_packing, receiver_only, extra_stack_offset,
5548                             sig_bt, sig_cc,
5549                             args_passed, args_on_stack, regs,
5550                             args_passed_to, args_on_stack_to, regs_to,
5551                             sp_inc, ret_off);
5552 }
5553 
5554 VMReg MacroAssembler::spill_reg_for(VMReg reg) {
5555   return reg->is_XMMRegister() ? xmm8->as_VMReg() : r14->as_VMReg();
5556 }
5557 
5558 void MacroAssembler::remove_frame(int initial_framesize, bool needs_stack_repair, int sp_inc_offset) {
5559   assert((initial_framesize & (StackAlignmentInBytes-1)) == 0, "frame size not aligned");
5560   if (needs_stack_repair) {
5561     movq(rbp, Address(rsp, initial_framesize));
5562     addq(rsp, Address(rsp, sp_inc_offset));
5563   } else {
5564     if (initial_framesize > 0) {
5565       addq(rsp, initial_framesize);
5566     }
5567     pop(rbp);
5568   }
5569 }
5570 
5571 void MacroAssembler::clear_mem(Register base, Register cnt, Register val, XMMRegister xtmp, bool is_large, bool word_copy_only) {
5572   // cnt - number of qwords (8-byte words).
5573   // base - start address, qword aligned.
5574   // is_large - if optimizers know cnt is larger than InitArrayShortSize
5575   assert(base==rdi, "base register must be edi for rep stos");
5576   assert(val==rax,   "tmp register must be eax for rep stos");
5577   assert(cnt==rcx,   "cnt register must be ecx for rep stos");
5578   assert(InitArrayShortSize % BytesPerLong == 0,
5579     "InitArrayShortSize should be the multiple of BytesPerLong");
5580 
5581   Label DONE;
5582 
5583   if (!is_large) {
5584     Label LOOP, LONG;
5585     cmpptr(cnt, InitArrayShortSize/BytesPerLong);
5586     jccb(Assembler::greater, LONG);
5587 
5588     NOT_LP64(shlptr(cnt, 1);) // convert to number of 32-bit words for 32-bit VM
5589 
5590     decrement(cnt);
5591     jccb(Assembler::negative, DONE); // Zero length
5592 
5593     // Use individual pointer-sized stores for small counts:
5594     BIND(LOOP);
5595     movptr(Address(base, cnt, Address::times_ptr), val);
5596     decrement(cnt);
5597     jccb(Assembler::greaterEqual, LOOP);
5598     jmpb(DONE);
5599 
5600     BIND(LONG);
5601   }
5602 
5603   // Use longer rep-prefixed ops for non-small counts:
5604   if (UseFastStosb && !word_copy_only) {
5605     shlptr(cnt, 3); // convert to number of bytes
5606     rep_stosb();
5607   } else if (UseXMMForObjInit) {
5608     xmm_clear_mem(base, cnt, val, xtmp);
5609   } else {
5610     NOT_LP64(shlptr(cnt, 1);) // convert to number of 32-bit words for 32-bit VM
5611     rep_stos();
5612   }
5613 
5614   BIND(DONE);
5615 }
5616 
5617 void MacroAssembler::generate_fill(BasicType t, bool aligned,
5618                                    Register to, Register value, Register count,
5619                                    Register rtmp, XMMRegister xtmp) {
5620   ShortBranchVerifier sbv(this);
5621   assert_different_registers(to, value, count, rtmp);
5622   Label L_exit;
5623   Label L_fill_2_bytes, L_fill_4_bytes;
5624 
5625   int shift = -1;
5626   switch (t) {
5627     case T_BYTE:
5628       shift = 2;
5629       break;
5630     case T_SHORT:
5631       shift = 1;
5632       break;
5633     case T_INT:
5634       shift = 0;
5635       break;
5636     default: ShouldNotReachHere();
5637   }
5638 
5639   if (t == T_BYTE) {
5640     andl(value, 0xff);
5641     movl(rtmp, value);
5642     shll(rtmp, 8);
5643     orl(value, rtmp);
5644   }
5645   if (t == T_SHORT) {
5646     andl(value, 0xffff);
5647   }
5648   if (t == T_BYTE || t == T_SHORT) {
5649     movl(rtmp, value);
5650     shll(rtmp, 16);
5651     orl(value, rtmp);
5652   }
5653 
5654   cmpl(count, 2<<shift); // Short arrays (< 8 bytes) fill by element
5655   jcc(Assembler::below, L_fill_4_bytes); // use unsigned cmp
5656   if (!UseUnalignedLoadStores && !aligned && (t == T_BYTE || t == T_SHORT)) {
5657     Label L_skip_align2;
5658     // align source address at 4 bytes address boundary
5659     if (t == T_BYTE) {
5660       Label L_skip_align1;
5661       // One byte misalignment happens only for byte arrays
5662       testptr(to, 1);
5663       jccb(Assembler::zero, L_skip_align1);
5664       movb(Address(to, 0), value);
5665       increment(to);
5666       decrement(count);
5667       BIND(L_skip_align1);
5668     }
5669     // Two bytes misalignment happens only for byte and short (char) arrays
5670     testptr(to, 2);
5671     jccb(Assembler::zero, L_skip_align2);
5672     movw(Address(to, 0), value);
5673     addptr(to, 2);
5674     subl(count, 1<<(shift-1));
5675     BIND(L_skip_align2);
5676   }
5677   if (UseSSE < 2) {
5678     Label L_fill_32_bytes_loop, L_check_fill_8_bytes, L_fill_8_bytes_loop, L_fill_8_bytes;
5679     // Fill 32-byte chunks
5680     subl(count, 8 << shift);
5681     jcc(Assembler::less, L_check_fill_8_bytes);
5682     align(16);
5683 
5684     BIND(L_fill_32_bytes_loop);
5685 
5686     for (int i = 0; i < 32; i += 4) {
5687       movl(Address(to, i), value);
5688     }
5689 
5690     addptr(to, 32);
5691     subl(count, 8 << shift);
5692     jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_fill_32_bytes_loop);
5693     BIND(L_check_fill_8_bytes);
5694     addl(count, 8 << shift);
5695     jccb(Assembler::zero, L_exit);
5696     jmpb(L_fill_8_bytes);
5697 
5698     //
5699     // length is too short, just fill qwords
5700     //
5701     BIND(L_fill_8_bytes_loop);
5702     movl(Address(to, 0), value);
5703     movl(Address(to, 4), value);
5704     addptr(to, 8);
5705     BIND(L_fill_8_bytes);
5706     subl(count, 1 << (shift + 1));
5707     jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_fill_8_bytes_loop);
5708     // fall through to fill 4 bytes
5709   } else {
5710     Label L_fill_32_bytes;
5711     if (!UseUnalignedLoadStores) {
5712       // align to 8 bytes, we know we are 4 byte aligned to start
5713       testptr(to, 4);
5714       jccb(Assembler::zero, L_fill_32_bytes);
5715       movl(Address(to, 0), value);
5716       addptr(to, 4);
5717       subl(count, 1<<shift);
5718     }
5719     BIND(L_fill_32_bytes);
5720     {
5721       assert( UseSSE >= 2, "supported cpu only" );
5722       Label L_fill_32_bytes_loop, L_check_fill_8_bytes, L_fill_8_bytes_loop, L_fill_8_bytes;
5723       movdl(xtmp, value);
5724       if (UseAVX >= 2 && UseUnalignedLoadStores) {
5725         Label L_check_fill_32_bytes;
5726         if (UseAVX > 2) {
5727           // Fill 64-byte chunks
5728           Label L_fill_64_bytes_loop_avx3, L_check_fill_64_bytes_avx2;
5729 
5730           // If number of bytes to fill < AVX3Threshold, perform fill using AVX2
5731           cmpl(count, AVX3Threshold);
5732           jccb(Assembler::below, L_check_fill_64_bytes_avx2);
5733 
5734           vpbroadcastd(xtmp, xtmp, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
5735 
5736           subl(count, 16 << shift);
5737           jccb(Assembler::less, L_check_fill_32_bytes);
5738           align(16);
5739 
5740           BIND(L_fill_64_bytes_loop_avx3);
5741           evmovdqul(Address(to, 0), xtmp, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
5742           addptr(to, 64);
5743           subl(count, 16 << shift);
5744           jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_fill_64_bytes_loop_avx3);
5745           jmpb(L_check_fill_32_bytes);
5746 
5747           BIND(L_check_fill_64_bytes_avx2);
5748         }
5749         // Fill 64-byte chunks
5750         Label L_fill_64_bytes_loop;
5751         vpbroadcastd(xtmp, xtmp, Assembler::AVX_256bit);
5752 
5753         subl(count, 16 << shift);
5754         jcc(Assembler::less, L_check_fill_32_bytes);
5755         align(16);
5756 
5757         BIND(L_fill_64_bytes_loop);
5758         vmovdqu(Address(to, 0), xtmp);
5759         vmovdqu(Address(to, 32), xtmp);
5760         addptr(to, 64);
5761         subl(count, 16 << shift);
5762         jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_fill_64_bytes_loop);
5763 
5764         BIND(L_check_fill_32_bytes);
5765         addl(count, 8 << shift);
5766         jccb(Assembler::less, L_check_fill_8_bytes);
5767         vmovdqu(Address(to, 0), xtmp);
5768         addptr(to, 32);
5769         subl(count, 8 << shift);
5770 
5771         BIND(L_check_fill_8_bytes);
5772         // clean upper bits of YMM registers
5773         movdl(xtmp, value);
5774         pshufd(xtmp, xtmp, 0);
5775       } else {
5776         // Fill 32-byte chunks
5777         pshufd(xtmp, xtmp, 0);
5778 
5779         subl(count, 8 << shift);
5780         jcc(Assembler::less, L_check_fill_8_bytes);
5781         align(16);
5782 
5783         BIND(L_fill_32_bytes_loop);
5784 
5785         if (UseUnalignedLoadStores) {
5786           movdqu(Address(to, 0), xtmp);
5787           movdqu(Address(to, 16), xtmp);
5788         } else {
5789           movq(Address(to, 0), xtmp);
5790           movq(Address(to, 8), xtmp);
5791           movq(Address(to, 16), xtmp);
5792           movq(Address(to, 24), xtmp);
5793         }
5794 
5795         addptr(to, 32);
5796         subl(count, 8 << shift);
5797         jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_fill_32_bytes_loop);
5798 
5799         BIND(L_check_fill_8_bytes);
5800       }
5801       addl(count, 8 << shift);
5802       jccb(Assembler::zero, L_exit);
5803       jmpb(L_fill_8_bytes);
5804 
5805       //
5806       // length is too short, just fill qwords
5807       //
5808       BIND(L_fill_8_bytes_loop);
5809       movq(Address(to, 0), xtmp);
5810       addptr(to, 8);
5811       BIND(L_fill_8_bytes);
5812       subl(count, 1 << (shift + 1));
5813       jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_fill_8_bytes_loop);
5814     }
5815   }
5816   // fill trailing 4 bytes
5817   BIND(L_fill_4_bytes);
5818   testl(count, 1<<shift);
5819   jccb(Assembler::zero, L_fill_2_bytes);
5820   movl(Address(to, 0), value);
5821   if (t == T_BYTE || t == T_SHORT) {
5822     Label L_fill_byte;
5823     addptr(to, 4);
5824     BIND(L_fill_2_bytes);
5825     // fill trailing 2 bytes
5826     testl(count, 1<<(shift-1));
5827     jccb(Assembler::zero, L_fill_byte);
5828     movw(Address(to, 0), value);
5829     if (t == T_BYTE) {
5830       addptr(to, 2);
5831       BIND(L_fill_byte);
5832       // fill trailing byte
5833       testl(count, 1);
5834       jccb(Assembler::zero, L_exit);
5835       movb(Address(to, 0), value);
5836     } else {
5837       BIND(L_fill_byte);
5838     }
5839   } else {
5840     BIND(L_fill_2_bytes);
5841   }
5842   BIND(L_exit);
5843 }
5844 
5845 // encode char[] to byte[] in ISO_8859_1
5846    //@HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate
5847    //private static int implEncodeISOArray(byte[] sa, int sp,
5848    //byte[] da, int dp, int len) {
5849    //  int i = 0;
5850    //  for (; i < len; i++) {
5851    //    char c = StringUTF16.getChar(sa, sp++);
5852    //    if (c > '\u00FF')
5853    //      break;
5854    //    da[dp++] = (byte)c;
5855    //  }
5856    //  return i;
5857    //}
5858 void MacroAssembler::encode_iso_array(Register src, Register dst, Register len,
5859   XMMRegister tmp1Reg, XMMRegister tmp2Reg,
5860   XMMRegister tmp3Reg, XMMRegister tmp4Reg,
5861   Register tmp5, Register result) {
5862 
5863   // rsi: src
5864   // rdi: dst
5865   // rdx: len
5866   // rcx: tmp5
5867   // rax: result
5868   ShortBranchVerifier sbv(this);
5869   assert_different_registers(src, dst, len, tmp5, result);
5870   Label L_done, L_copy_1_char, L_copy_1_char_exit;
5871 
5872   // set result
5873   xorl(result, result);
5874   // check for zero length
5875   testl(len, len);
5876   jcc(Assembler::zero, L_done);
5877 
5878   movl(result, len);
5879 
5880   // Setup pointers
5881   lea(src, Address(src, len, Address::times_2)); // char[]
5882   lea(dst, Address(dst, len, Address::times_1)); // byte[]
5883   negptr(len);
5884 
5885   if (UseSSE42Intrinsics || UseAVX >= 2) {
5886     Label L_copy_8_chars, L_copy_8_chars_exit;
5887     Label L_chars_16_check, L_copy_16_chars, L_copy_16_chars_exit;
5888 
5889     if (UseAVX >= 2) {
5890       Label L_chars_32_check, L_copy_32_chars, L_copy_32_chars_exit;
5891       movl(tmp5, 0xff00ff00);   // create mask to test for Unicode chars in vector
5892       movdl(tmp1Reg, tmp5);
5893       vpbroadcastd(tmp1Reg, tmp1Reg, Assembler::AVX_256bit);
5894       jmp(L_chars_32_check);
5895 
5896       bind(L_copy_32_chars);
5897       vmovdqu(tmp3Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -64));
5898       vmovdqu(tmp4Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -32));
5899       vpor(tmp2Reg, tmp3Reg, tmp4Reg, /* vector_len */ 1);
5900       vptest(tmp2Reg, tmp1Reg);       // check for Unicode chars in  vector
5901       jccb(Assembler::notZero, L_copy_32_chars_exit);
5902       vpackuswb(tmp3Reg, tmp3Reg, tmp4Reg, /* vector_len */ 1);
5903       vpermq(tmp4Reg, tmp3Reg, 0xD8, /* vector_len */ 1);
5904       vmovdqu(Address(dst, len, Address::times_1, -32), tmp4Reg);
5905 
5906       bind(L_chars_32_check);
5907       addptr(len, 32);
5908       jcc(Assembler::lessEqual, L_copy_32_chars);
5909 
5910       bind(L_copy_32_chars_exit);
5911       subptr(len, 16);
5912       jccb(Assembler::greater, L_copy_16_chars_exit);
5913 
5914     } else if (UseSSE42Intrinsics) {
5915       movl(tmp5, 0xff00ff00);   // create mask to test for Unicode chars in vector
5916       movdl(tmp1Reg, tmp5);
5917       pshufd(tmp1Reg, tmp1Reg, 0);
5918       jmpb(L_chars_16_check);
5919     }
5920 
5921     bind(L_copy_16_chars);
5922     if (UseAVX >= 2) {
5923       vmovdqu(tmp2Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -32));
5924       vptest(tmp2Reg, tmp1Reg);
5925       jcc(Assembler::notZero, L_copy_16_chars_exit);
5926       vpackuswb(tmp2Reg, tmp2Reg, tmp1Reg, /* vector_len */ 1);
5927       vpermq(tmp3Reg, tmp2Reg, 0xD8, /* vector_len */ 1);
5928     } else {
5929       if (UseAVX > 0) {
5930         movdqu(tmp3Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -32));
5931         movdqu(tmp4Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -16));
5932         vpor(tmp2Reg, tmp3Reg, tmp4Reg, /* vector_len */ 0);
5933       } else {
5934         movdqu(tmp3Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -32));
5935         por(tmp2Reg, tmp3Reg);
5936         movdqu(tmp4Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -16));
5937         por(tmp2Reg, tmp4Reg);
5938       }
5939       ptest(tmp2Reg, tmp1Reg);       // check for Unicode chars in  vector
5940       jccb(Assembler::notZero, L_copy_16_chars_exit);
5941       packuswb(tmp3Reg, tmp4Reg);
5942     }
5943     movdqu(Address(dst, len, Address::times_1, -16), tmp3Reg);
5944 
5945     bind(L_chars_16_check);
5946     addptr(len, 16);
5947     jcc(Assembler::lessEqual, L_copy_16_chars);
5948 
5949     bind(L_copy_16_chars_exit);
5950     if (UseAVX >= 2) {
5951       // clean upper bits of YMM registers
5952       vpxor(tmp2Reg, tmp2Reg);
5953       vpxor(tmp3Reg, tmp3Reg);
5954       vpxor(tmp4Reg, tmp4Reg);
5955       movdl(tmp1Reg, tmp5);
5956       pshufd(tmp1Reg, tmp1Reg, 0);
5957     }
5958     subptr(len, 8);
5959     jccb(Assembler::greater, L_copy_8_chars_exit);
5960 
5961     bind(L_copy_8_chars);
5962     movdqu(tmp3Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, -16));
5963     ptest(tmp3Reg, tmp1Reg);
5964     jccb(Assembler::notZero, L_copy_8_chars_exit);
5965     packuswb(tmp3Reg, tmp1Reg);
5966     movq(Address(dst, len, Address::times_1, -8), tmp3Reg);
5967     addptr(len, 8);
5968     jccb(Assembler::lessEqual, L_copy_8_chars);
5969 
5970     bind(L_copy_8_chars_exit);
5971     subptr(len, 8);
5972     jccb(Assembler::zero, L_done);
5973   }
5974 
5975   bind(L_copy_1_char);
5976   load_unsigned_short(tmp5, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, 0));
5977   testl(tmp5, 0xff00);      // check if Unicode char
5978   jccb(Assembler::notZero, L_copy_1_char_exit);
5979   movb(Address(dst, len, Address::times_1, 0), tmp5);
5980   addptr(len, 1);
5981   jccb(Assembler::less, L_copy_1_char);
5982 
5983   bind(L_copy_1_char_exit);
5984   addptr(result, len); // len is negative count of not processed elements
5985 
5986   bind(L_done);
5987 }
