5989 #ifdef _LP64
5990 /**
5991  * Helper for multiply_to_len().
5992  */
5993 void MacroAssembler::add2_with_carry(Register dest_hi, Register dest_lo, Register src1, Register src2) {
5994   addq(dest_lo, src1);
5995   adcq(dest_hi, 0);
5996   addq(dest_lo, src2);
5997   adcq(dest_hi, 0);
5998 }
5999 
6000 /**
6001  * Multiply 64 bit by 64 bit first loop.
6002  */
6003 void MacroAssembler::multiply_64_x_64_loop(Register x, Register xstart, Register x_xstart,
6004                                            Register y, Register y_idx, Register z,
6005                                            Register carry, Register product,
6006                                            Register idx, Register kdx) {
6007   //
6008   //  jlong carry, x[], y[], z[];
6009   //  for (int idx=ystart, kdx=ystart+1+xstart; idx >= 0; idx-, kdx--) {
6010   //    huge_128 product = y[idx] * x[xstart] + carry;
6011   //    z[kdx] = (jlong)product;
6012   //    carry  = (jlong)(product >>> 64);
6013   //  }
6014   //  z[xstart] = carry;
6015   //
6016 
6017   Label L_first_loop, L_first_loop_exit;
6018   Label L_one_x, L_one_y, L_multiply;
6019 
6020   decrementl(xstart);
6021   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_one_x);
6022 
6023   movq(x_xstart, Address(x, xstart, Address::times_4,  0));
6024   rorq(x_xstart, 32); // convert big-endian to little-endian
6025 
6026   bind(L_first_loop);
6027   decrementl(idx);
6028   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_first_loop_exit);
6029   decrementl(idx);
6030   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_one_y);
6031   movq(y_idx, Address(y, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6032   rorq(y_idx, 32); // convert big-endian to little-endian
6033   bind(L_multiply);
6034   movq(product, x_xstart);
6035   mulq(y_idx); // product(rax) * y_idx -> rdx:rax
6036   addq(product, carry);
6037   adcq(rdx, 0);
6038   subl(kdx, 2);
6039   movl(Address(z, kdx, Address::times_4,  4), product);
6040   shrq(product, 32);
6041   movl(Address(z, kdx, Address::times_4,  0), product);
6042   movq(carry, rdx);
6043   jmp(L_first_loop);
6044 
6045   bind(L_one_y);
6046   movl(y_idx, Address(y,  0));
6047   jmp(L_multiply);
6048 
6049   bind(L_one_x);
6050   movl(x_xstart, Address(x,  0));
6051   jmp(L_first_loop);
6052 
6053   bind(L_first_loop_exit);
6054 }
6055 
6056 /**
6057  * Multiply 64 bit by 64 bit and add 128 bit.
6058  */
6059 void MacroAssembler::multiply_add_128_x_128(Register x_xstart, Register y, Register z,
6060                                             Register yz_idx, Register idx,
6061                                             Register carry, Register product, int offset) {
6062   //     huge_128 product = (y[idx] * x_xstart) + z[kdx] + carry;
6063   //     z[kdx] = (jlong)product;
6064 
6065   movq(yz_idx, Address(y, idx, Address::times_4,  offset));
6066   rorq(yz_idx, 32); // convert big-endian to little-endian
6067   movq(product, x_xstart);
6068   mulq(yz_idx);     // product(rax) * yz_idx -> rdx:product(rax)
6069   movq(yz_idx, Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  offset));
6070   rorq(yz_idx, 32); // convert big-endian to little-endian
6071 
6072   add2_with_carry(rdx, product, carry, yz_idx);
6073 
6074   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  offset+4), product);
6075   shrq(product, 32);
6076   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  offset), product);
6077 
6078 }
6079 
6080 /**
6081  * Multiply 128 bit by 128 bit. Unrolled inner loop.
6082  */
6083 void MacroAssembler::multiply_128_x_128_loop(Register x_xstart, Register y, Register z,
6084                                              Register yz_idx, Register idx, Register jdx,
6085                                              Register carry, Register product,
6086                                              Register carry2) {
6087   //   jlong carry, x[], y[], z[];
6088   //   int kdx = ystart+1;
6089   //   for (int idx=ystart-2; idx >= 0; idx -= 2) { // Third loop
6090   //     huge_128 product = (y[idx+1] * x_xstart) + z[kdx+idx+1] + carry;
6091   //     z[kdx+idx+1] = (jlong)product;
6092   //     jlong carry2  = (jlong)(product >>> 64);
6093   //     product = (y[idx] * x_xstart) + z[kdx+idx] + carry2;
6094   //     z[kdx+idx] = (jlong)product;
6095   //     carry  = (jlong)(product >>> 64);
6096   //   }
6097   //   idx += 2;
6098   //   if (idx > 0) {
6099   //     product = (y[idx] * x_xstart) + z[kdx+idx] + carry;
6100   //     z[kdx+idx] = (jlong)product;
6101   //     carry  = (jlong)(product >>> 64);
6102   //   }
6103   //
6104 
6105   Label L_third_loop, L_third_loop_exit, L_post_third_loop_done;
6106 
6107   movl(jdx, idx);
6108   andl(jdx, 0xFFFFFFFC);
6109   shrl(jdx, 2);
6110 
6111   bind(L_third_loop);
6112   subl(jdx, 1);
6113   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_third_loop_exit);
6114   subl(idx, 4);
6115 
6116   multiply_add_128_x_128(x_xstart, y, z, yz_idx, idx, carry, product, 8);
6117   movq(carry2, rdx);
6118 
6119   multiply_add_128_x_128(x_xstart, y, z, yz_idx, idx, carry2, product, 0);
6120   movq(carry, rdx);
6121   jmp(L_third_loop);
6122 
6123   bind (L_third_loop_exit);
6124 
6125   andl (idx, 0x3);
6126   jcc(Assembler::zero, L_post_third_loop_done);
6127 
6128   Label L_check_1;
6129   subl(idx, 2);
6130   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_check_1);
6131 
6132   multiply_add_128_x_128(x_xstart, y, z, yz_idx, idx, carry, product, 0);
6133   movq(carry, rdx);
6134 
6135   bind (L_check_1);
6136   addl (idx, 0x2);
6137   andl (idx, 0x1);
6138   subl(idx, 1);
6139   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_post_third_loop_done);
6140 
6141   movl(yz_idx, Address(y, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6142   movq(product, x_xstart);
6143   mulq(yz_idx); // product(rax) * yz_idx -> rdx:product(rax)
6144   movl(yz_idx, Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6145 
6146   add2_with_carry(rdx, product, yz_idx, carry);
6147 
6148   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0), product);
6149   shrq(product, 32);
6150 
6151   shlq(rdx, 32);
6152   orq(product, rdx);
6153   movq(carry, product);
6154 
6155   bind(L_post_third_loop_done);
6156 }
6157 
6158 /**
6159  * Multiply 128 bit by 128 bit using BMI2. Unrolled inner loop.
6160  *
6161  */
6162 void MacroAssembler::multiply_128_x_128_bmi2_loop(Register y, Register z,
6163                                                   Register carry, Register carry2,
6164                                                   Register idx, Register jdx,
6165                                                   Register yz_idx1, Register yz_idx2,
6166                                                   Register tmp, Register tmp3, Register tmp4) {
6167   assert(UseBMI2Instructions, "should be used only when BMI2 is available");
6168 
6169   //   jlong carry, x[], y[], z[];
6170   //   int kdx = ystart+1;
6171   //   for (int idx=ystart-2; idx >= 0; idx -= 2) { // Third loop
6172   //     huge_128 tmp3 = (y[idx+1] * rdx) + z[kdx+idx+1] + carry;
6173   //     jlong carry2  = (jlong)(tmp3 >>> 64);
6174   //     huge_128 tmp4 = (y[idx]   * rdx) + z[kdx+idx] + carry2;
6175   //     carry  = (jlong)(tmp4 >>> 64);
6176   //     z[kdx+idx+1] = (jlong)tmp3;
6177   //     z[kdx+idx] = (jlong)tmp4;
6178   //   }
6179   //   idx += 2;
6180   //   if (idx > 0) {
6181   //     yz_idx1 = (y[idx] * rdx) + z[kdx+idx] + carry;
6182   //     z[kdx+idx] = (jlong)yz_idx1;
6183   //     carry  = (jlong)(yz_idx1 >>> 64);
6184   //   }
6185   //
6186 
6187   Label L_third_loop, L_third_loop_exit, L_post_third_loop_done;
6188 
6189   movl(jdx, idx);
6190   andl(jdx, 0xFFFFFFFC);
6191   shrl(jdx, 2);
6192 
6193   bind(L_third_loop);
6194   subl(jdx, 1);
6195   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_third_loop_exit);
6196   subl(idx, 4);
6197 
6198   movq(yz_idx1,  Address(y, idx, Address::times_4,  8));
6199   rorxq(yz_idx1, yz_idx1, 32); // convert big-endian to little-endian
6200   movq(yz_idx2, Address(y, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6201   rorxq(yz_idx2, yz_idx2, 32);
6202 
6203   mulxq(tmp4, tmp3, yz_idx1);  //  yz_idx1 * rdx -> tmp4:tmp3
6204   mulxq(carry2, tmp, yz_idx2); //  yz_idx2 * rdx -> carry2:tmp
6205 
6206   movq(yz_idx1,  Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  8));
6207   rorxq(yz_idx1, yz_idx1, 32);
6208   movq(yz_idx2, Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6209   rorxq(yz_idx2, yz_idx2, 32);
6210 
6211   if (VM_Version::supports_adx()) {
6212     adcxq(tmp3, carry);
6213     adoxq(tmp3, yz_idx1);
6214 
6215     adcxq(tmp4, tmp);
6216     adoxq(tmp4, yz_idx2);
6217 
6218     movl(carry, 0); // does not affect flags
6219     adcxq(carry2, carry);
6220     adoxq(carry2, carry);
6221   } else {
6222     add2_with_carry(tmp4, tmp3, carry, yz_idx1);
6223     add2_with_carry(carry2, tmp4, tmp, yz_idx2);
6224   }
6225   movq(carry, carry2);
6226 
6227   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4, 12), tmp3);
6228   shrq(tmp3, 32);
6229   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  8), tmp3);
6230 
6231   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  4), tmp4);
6232   shrq(tmp4, 32);
6233   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0), tmp4);
6234 
6235   jmp(L_third_loop);
6236 
6237   bind (L_third_loop_exit);
6238 
6239   andl (idx, 0x3);
6240   jcc(Assembler::zero, L_post_third_loop_done);
6241 
6242   Label L_check_1;
6243   subl(idx, 2);
6244   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_check_1);
6245 
6246   movq(yz_idx1, Address(y, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6247   rorxq(yz_idx1, yz_idx1, 32);
6248   mulxq(tmp4, tmp3, yz_idx1); //  yz_idx1 * rdx -> tmp4:tmp3
6249   movq(yz_idx2, Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6250   rorxq(yz_idx2, yz_idx2, 32);
6251 
6252   add2_with_carry(tmp4, tmp3, carry, yz_idx2);
6253 
6254   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  4), tmp3);
6255   shrq(tmp3, 32);
6256   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0), tmp3);
6257   movq(carry, tmp4);
6258 
6259   bind (L_check_1);
6260   addl (idx, 0x2);
6261   andl (idx, 0x1);
6262   subl(idx, 1);
6263   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_post_third_loop_done);
6264   movl(tmp4, Address(y, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6265   mulxq(carry2, tmp3, tmp4);  //  tmp4 * rdx -> carry2:tmp3
6266   movl(tmp4, Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0));
6267 
6268   add2_with_carry(carry2, tmp3, tmp4, carry);
6269 
6270   movl(Address(z, idx, Address::times_4,  0), tmp3);
6271   shrq(tmp3, 32);
6272 
6273   shlq(carry2, 32);
6274   orq(tmp3, carry2);
6275   movq(carry, tmp3);
6276 
6277   bind(L_post_third_loop_done);
6278 }
6279 
6280 /**
6281  * Code for BigInteger::multiplyToLen() instrinsic.
6282  *
6283  * rdi: x
6284  * rax: xlen
6285  * rsi: y
6286  * rcx: ylen
6287  * r8:  z
6288  * r11: zlen
6289  * r12: tmp1
6290  * r13: tmp2
6291  * r14: tmp3
6292  * r15: tmp4
6293  * rbx: tmp5
6294  *
6295  */
6296 void MacroAssembler::multiply_to_len(Register x, Register xlen, Register y, Register ylen, Register z, Register zlen,
6297                                      Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3, Register tmp4, Register tmp5) {
6298   ShortBranchVerifier sbv(this);
6299   assert_different_registers(x, xlen, y, ylen, z, zlen, tmp1, tmp2, tmp3, tmp4, tmp5, rdx);
6300 
6301   push(tmp1);
6302   push(tmp2);
6303   push(tmp3);
6304   push(tmp4);
6305   push(tmp5);
6306 
6307   push(xlen);
6308   push(zlen);
6309 
6310   const Register idx = tmp1;
6311   const Register kdx = tmp2;
6312   const Register xstart = tmp3;
6313 
6314   const Register y_idx = tmp4;
6315   const Register carry = tmp5;
6316   const Register product  = xlen;
6317   const Register x_xstart = zlen;  // reuse register
6318 
6319   // First Loop.
6320   //
6321   //  final static long LONG_MASK = 0xffffffffL;
6322   //  int xstart = xlen - 1;
6323   //  int ystart = ylen - 1;
6324   //  long carry = 0;
6325   //  for (int idx=ystart, kdx=ystart+1+xstart; idx >= 0; idx-, kdx--) {
6326   //    long product = (y[idx] & LONG_MASK) * (x[xstart] & LONG_MASK) + carry;
6327   //    z[kdx] = (int)product;
6328   //    carry = product >>> 32;
6329   //  }
6330   //  z[xstart] = (int)carry;
6331   //
6332 
6333   movl(idx, ylen);      // idx = ylen;
6334   movl(kdx, zlen);      // kdx = xlen+ylen;
6335   xorq(carry, carry);   // carry = 0;
6336 
6337   Label L_done;
6338 
6339   movl(xstart, xlen);
6340   decrementl(xstart);
6341   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_done);
6342 
6343   multiply_64_x_64_loop(x, xstart, x_xstart, y, y_idx, z, carry, product, idx, kdx);
6344 
6345   Label L_second_loop;
6346   testl(kdx, kdx);
6347   jcc(Assembler::zero, L_second_loop);
6348 
6349   Label L_carry;
6350   subl(kdx, 1);
6351   jcc(Assembler::zero, L_carry);
6352 
6353   movl(Address(z, kdx, Address::times_4,  0), carry);
6354   shrq(carry, 32);
6355   subl(kdx, 1);
6356 
6357   bind(L_carry);
6358   movl(Address(z, kdx, Address::times_4,  0), carry);
6359 
6360   // Second and third (nested) loops.
6361   //
6362   // for (int i = xstart-1; i >= 0; i--) { // Second loop
6363   //   carry = 0;
6364   //   for (int jdx=ystart, k=ystart+1+i; jdx >= 0; jdx--, k--) { // Third loop
6365   //     long product = (y[jdx] & LONG_MASK) * (x[i] & LONG_MASK) +
6366   //                    (z[k] & LONG_MASK) + carry;
6367   //     z[k] = (int)product;
6368   //     carry = product >>> 32;
6369   //   }
6370   //   z[i] = (int)carry;
6371   // }
6372   //
6373   // i = xlen, j = tmp1, k = tmp2, carry = tmp5, x[i] = rdx
6374 
6375   const Register jdx = tmp1;
6376 
6377   bind(L_second_loop);
6378   xorl(carry, carry);    // carry = 0;
6379   movl(jdx, ylen);       // j = ystart+1
6380 
6381   subl(xstart, 1);       // i = xstart-1;
6382   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_done);
6383 
6384   push (z);
6385 
6386   Label L_last_x;
6387   lea(z, Address(z, xstart, Address::times_4, 4)); // z = z + k - j
6388   subl(xstart, 1);       // i = xstart-1;
6389   jcc(Assembler::negative, L_last_x);
6390 
6391   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
6392     movq(rdx,  Address(x, xstart, Address::times_4,  0));
6393     rorxq(rdx, rdx, 32); // convert big-endian to little-endian
6394   } else {
6395     movq(x_xstart, Address(x, xstart, Address::times_4,  0));
6396     rorq(x_xstart, 32);  // convert big-endian to little-endian
6397   }
6398 
6399   Label L_third_loop_prologue;
6400   bind(L_third_loop_prologue);
6401 
6402   push (x);
6403   push (xstart);
6404   push (ylen);
6405 
6406 
6407   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
6408     multiply_128_x_128_bmi2_loop(y, z, carry, x, jdx, ylen, product, tmp2, x_xstart, tmp3, tmp4);
6409   } else { // !UseBMI2Instructions
6410     multiply_128_x_128_loop(x_xstart, y, z, y_idx, jdx, ylen, carry, product, x);
6411   }
6412 
6413   pop(ylen);
6414   pop(xlen);
6415   pop(x);
6416   pop(z);
6417 
6418   movl(tmp3, xlen);
6419   addl(tmp3, 1);
6420   movl(Address(z, tmp3, Address::times_4,  0), carry);
6421   subl(tmp3, 1);
6422   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_done);
6423 
6424   shrq(carry, 32);
6425   movl(Address(z, tmp3, Address::times_4,  0), carry);
6426   jmp(L_second_loop);
6427 
6428   // Next infrequent code is moved outside loops.
6429   bind(L_last_x);
6430   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
6431     movl(rdx, Address(x,  0));
6432   } else {
6433     movl(x_xstart, Address(x,  0));
6434   }
6435   jmp(L_third_loop_prologue);
6436 
6437   bind(L_done);
6438 
6439   pop(zlen);
6440   pop(xlen);
6441 
6442   pop(tmp5);
6443   pop(tmp4);
6444   pop(tmp3);
6445   pop(tmp2);
6446   pop(tmp1);
6447 }
6448 
6449 void MacroAssembler::vectorized_mismatch(Register obja, Register objb, Register length, Register log2_array_indxscale,
6450   Register result, Register tmp1, Register tmp2, XMMRegister rymm0, XMMRegister rymm1, XMMRegister rymm2){
6451   assert(UseSSE42Intrinsics, "SSE4.2 must be enabled.");
6452   Label VECTOR16_LOOP, VECTOR8_LOOP, VECTOR4_LOOP;
6453   Label VECTOR8_TAIL, VECTOR4_TAIL;
6454   Label VECTOR32_NOT_EQUAL, VECTOR16_NOT_EQUAL, VECTOR8_NOT_EQUAL, VECTOR4_NOT_EQUAL;
6455   Label SAME_TILL_END, DONE;
6456   Label BYTES_LOOP, BYTES_TAIL, BYTES_NOT_EQUAL;
6457 
6458   //scale is in rcx in both Win64 and Unix
6459   ShortBranchVerifier sbv(this);
6460 
6461   shlq(length);
6462   xorq(result, result);
6463 
6464   if ((AVX3Threshold == 0) && (UseAVX > 2) &&
6465       VM_Version::supports_avx512vlbw()) {
6466     Label VECTOR64_LOOP, VECTOR64_NOT_EQUAL, VECTOR32_TAIL;
6467 
6468     cmpq(length, 64);
6469     jcc(Assembler::less, VECTOR32_TAIL);
6470 
6471     movq(tmp1, length);
6472     andq(tmp1, 0x3F);      // tail count
6473     andq(length, ~(0x3F)); //vector count
6474 
6475     bind(VECTOR64_LOOP);
6476     // AVX512 code to compare 64 byte vectors.
6477     evmovdqub(rymm0, Address(obja, result), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
6478     evpcmpeqb(k7, rymm0, Address(objb, result), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
6479     kortestql(k7, k7);
6480     jcc(Assembler::aboveEqual, VECTOR64_NOT_EQUAL);     // mismatch
6481     addq(result, 64);
6482     subq(length, 64);
6483     jccb(Assembler::notZero, VECTOR64_LOOP);
6484 
6485     //bind(VECTOR64_TAIL);
6486     testq(tmp1, tmp1);
6487     jcc(Assembler::zero, SAME_TILL_END);
6488 
6489     //bind(VECTOR64_TAIL);
6490     // AVX512 code to compare upto 63 byte vectors.
6491     mov64(tmp2, 0xFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFF);
6492     shlxq(tmp2, tmp2, tmp1);
6493     notq(tmp2);
6494     kmovql(k3, tmp2);
6495 
6496     evmovdqub(rymm0, k3, Address(obja, result), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
6497     evpcmpeqb(k7, k3, rymm0, Address(objb, result), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
6498 
6499     ktestql(k7, k3);
6500     jcc(Assembler::below, SAME_TILL_END);     // not mismatch
6501 
6502     bind(VECTOR64_NOT_EQUAL);
6503     kmovql(tmp1, k7);
6504     notq(tmp1);
6505     tzcntq(tmp1, tmp1);
6506     addq(result, tmp1);
6507     shrq(result);
6508     jmp(DONE);
6509     bind(VECTOR32_TAIL);
6510   }
6511 
6512   cmpq(length, 8);
6513   jcc(Assembler::equal, VECTOR8_LOOP);
6514   jcc(Assembler::less, VECTOR4_TAIL);
6515 
6516   if (UseAVX >= 2) {
6517     Label VECTOR16_TAIL, VECTOR32_LOOP;
6518 
6519     cmpq(length, 16);
6520     jcc(Assembler::equal, VECTOR16_LOOP);
6521     jcc(Assembler::less, VECTOR8_LOOP);
6522 
6523     cmpq(length, 32);
6524     jccb(Assembler::less, VECTOR16_TAIL);
6525 
6526     subq(length, 32);
6527     bind(VECTOR32_LOOP);
6528     vmovdqu(rymm0, Address(obja, result));
6529     vmovdqu(rymm1, Address(objb, result));
6530     vpxor(rymm2, rymm0, rymm1, Assembler::AVX_256bit);
6531     vptest(rymm2, rymm2);
6532     jcc(Assembler::notZero, VECTOR32_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6533     addq(result, 32);
6534     subq(length, 32);
6535     jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, VECTOR32_LOOP);
6536     addq(length, 32);
6537     jcc(Assembler::equal, SAME_TILL_END);
6538     //falling through if less than 32 bytes left //close the branch here.
6539 
6540     bind(VECTOR16_TAIL);
6541     cmpq(length, 16);
6542     jccb(Assembler::less, VECTOR8_TAIL);
6543     bind(VECTOR16_LOOP);
6544     movdqu(rymm0, Address(obja, result));
6545     movdqu(rymm1, Address(objb, result));
6546     vpxor(rymm2, rymm0, rymm1, Assembler::AVX_128bit);
6547     ptest(rymm2, rymm2);
6548     jcc(Assembler::notZero, VECTOR16_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6549     addq(result, 16);
6550     subq(length, 16);
6551     jcc(Assembler::equal, SAME_TILL_END);
6552     //falling through if less than 16 bytes left
6553   } else {//regular intrinsics
6554 
6555     cmpq(length, 16);
6556     jccb(Assembler::less, VECTOR8_TAIL);
6557 
6558     subq(length, 16);
6559     bind(VECTOR16_LOOP);
6560     movdqu(rymm0, Address(obja, result));
6561     movdqu(rymm1, Address(objb, result));
6562     pxor(rymm0, rymm1);
6563     ptest(rymm0, rymm0);
6564     jcc(Assembler::notZero, VECTOR16_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6565     addq(result, 16);
6566     subq(length, 16);
6567     jccb(Assembler::greaterEqual, VECTOR16_LOOP);
6568     addq(length, 16);
6569     jcc(Assembler::equal, SAME_TILL_END);
6570     //falling through if less than 16 bytes left
6571   }
6572 
6573   bind(VECTOR8_TAIL);
6574   cmpq(length, 8);
6575   jccb(Assembler::less, VECTOR4_TAIL);
6576   bind(VECTOR8_LOOP);
6577   movq(tmp1, Address(obja, result));
6578   movq(tmp2, Address(objb, result));
6579   xorq(tmp1, tmp2);
6580   testq(tmp1, tmp1);
6581   jcc(Assembler::notZero, VECTOR8_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6582   addq(result, 8);
6583   subq(length, 8);
6584   jcc(Assembler::equal, SAME_TILL_END);
6585   //falling through if less than 8 bytes left
6586 
6587   bind(VECTOR4_TAIL);
6588   cmpq(length, 4);
6589   jccb(Assembler::less, BYTES_TAIL);
6590   bind(VECTOR4_LOOP);
6591   movl(tmp1, Address(obja, result));
6592   xorl(tmp1, Address(objb, result));
6593   testl(tmp1, tmp1);
6594   jcc(Assembler::notZero, VECTOR4_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6595   addq(result, 4);
6596   subq(length, 4);
6597   jcc(Assembler::equal, SAME_TILL_END);
6598   //falling through if less than 4 bytes left
6599 
6600   bind(BYTES_TAIL);
6601   bind(BYTES_LOOP);
6602   load_unsigned_byte(tmp1, Address(obja, result));
6603   load_unsigned_byte(tmp2, Address(objb, result));
6604   xorl(tmp1, tmp2);
6605   testl(tmp1, tmp1);
6606   jcc(Assembler::notZero, BYTES_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6607   decq(length);
6608   jcc(Assembler::zero, SAME_TILL_END);
6609   incq(result);
6610   load_unsigned_byte(tmp1, Address(obja, result));
6611   load_unsigned_byte(tmp2, Address(objb, result));
6612   xorl(tmp1, tmp2);
6613   testl(tmp1, tmp1);
6614   jcc(Assembler::notZero, BYTES_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6615   decq(length);
6616   jcc(Assembler::zero, SAME_TILL_END);
6617   incq(result);
6618   load_unsigned_byte(tmp1, Address(obja, result));
6619   load_unsigned_byte(tmp2, Address(objb, result));
6620   xorl(tmp1, tmp2);
6621   testl(tmp1, tmp1);
6622   jcc(Assembler::notZero, BYTES_NOT_EQUAL);//mismatch found
6623   jmp(SAME_TILL_END);
6624 
6625   if (UseAVX >= 2) {
6626     bind(VECTOR32_NOT_EQUAL);
6627     vpcmpeqb(rymm2, rymm2, rymm2, Assembler::AVX_256bit);
6628     vpcmpeqb(rymm0, rymm0, rymm1, Assembler::AVX_256bit);
6629     vpxor(rymm0, rymm0, rymm2, Assembler::AVX_256bit);
6630     vpmovmskb(tmp1, rymm0);
6631     bsfq(tmp1, tmp1);
6632     addq(result, tmp1);
6633     shrq(result);
6634     jmp(DONE);
6635   }
6636 
6637   bind(VECTOR16_NOT_EQUAL);
6638   if (UseAVX >= 2) {
6639     vpcmpeqb(rymm2, rymm2, rymm2, Assembler::AVX_128bit);
6640     vpcmpeqb(rymm0, rymm0, rymm1, Assembler::AVX_128bit);
6641     pxor(rymm0, rymm2);
6642   } else {
6643     pcmpeqb(rymm2, rymm2);
6644     pxor(rymm0, rymm1);
6645     pcmpeqb(rymm0, rymm1);
6646     pxor(rymm0, rymm2);
6647   }
6648   pmovmskb(tmp1, rymm0);
6649   bsfq(tmp1, tmp1);
6650   addq(result, tmp1);
6651   shrq(result);
6652   jmpb(DONE);
6653 
6654   bind(VECTOR8_NOT_EQUAL);
6655   bind(VECTOR4_NOT_EQUAL);
6656   bsfq(tmp1, tmp1);
6657   shrq(tmp1, 3);
6658   addq(result, tmp1);
6659   bind(BYTES_NOT_EQUAL);
6660   shrq(result);
6661   jmpb(DONE);
6662 
6663   bind(SAME_TILL_END);
6664   mov64(result, -1);
6665 
6666   bind(DONE);
6667 }
6668 
6669 //Helper functions for square_to_len()
6670 
6671 /**
6672  * Store the squares of x[], right shifted one bit (divided by 2) into z[]
6673  * Preserves x and z and modifies rest of the registers.
6674  */
6675 void MacroAssembler::square_rshift(Register x, Register xlen, Register z, Register tmp1, Register tmp3, Register tmp4, Register tmp5, Register rdxReg, Register raxReg) {
6676   // Perform square and right shift by 1
6677   // Handle odd xlen case first, then for even xlen do the following
6678   // jlong carry = 0;
6679   // for (int j=0, i=0; j < xlen; j+=2, i+=4) {
6680   //     huge_128 product = x[j:j+1] * x[j:j+1];
6681   //     z[i:i+1] = (carry << 63) | (jlong)(product >>> 65);
6682   //     z[i+2:i+3] = (jlong)(product >>> 1);
6683   //     carry = (jlong)product;
6684   // }
6685 
6686   xorq(tmp5, tmp5);     // carry
6687   xorq(rdxReg, rdxReg);
6688   xorl(tmp1, tmp1);     // index for x
6689   xorl(tmp4, tmp4);     // index for z
6690 
6691   Label L_first_loop, L_first_loop_exit;
6692 
6693   testl(xlen, 1);
6694   jccb(Assembler::zero, L_first_loop); //jump if xlen is even
6695 
6696   // Square and right shift by 1 the odd element using 32 bit multiply
6697   movl(raxReg, Address(x, tmp1, Address::times_4, 0));
6698   imulq(raxReg, raxReg);
6699   shrq(raxReg, 1);
6700   adcq(tmp5, 0);
6701   movq(Address(z, tmp4, Address::times_4, 0), raxReg);
6702   incrementl(tmp1);
6703   addl(tmp4, 2);
6704 
6705   // Square and  right shift by 1 the rest using 64 bit multiply
6706   bind(L_first_loop);
6707   cmpptr(tmp1, xlen);
6708   jccb(Assembler::equal, L_first_loop_exit);
6709 
6710   // Square
6711   movq(raxReg, Address(x, tmp1, Address::times_4,  0));
6712   rorq(raxReg, 32);    // convert big-endian to little-endian
6713   mulq(raxReg);        // 64-bit multiply rax * rax -> rdx:rax
6714 
6715   // Right shift by 1 and save carry
6716   shrq(tmp5, 1);       // rdx:rax:tmp5 = (tmp5:rdx:rax) >>> 1
6717   rcrq(rdxReg, 1);
6718   rcrq(raxReg, 1);
6719   adcq(tmp5, 0);
6720 
6721   // Store result in z
6722   movq(Address(z, tmp4, Address::times_4, 0), rdxReg);
6723   movq(Address(z, tmp4, Address::times_4, 8), raxReg);
6724 
6725   // Update indices for x and z
6726   addl(tmp1, 2);
6727   addl(tmp4, 4);
6728   jmp(L_first_loop);
6729 
6730   bind(L_first_loop_exit);
6731 }
6732 
6733 
6734 /**
6735  * Perform the following multiply add operation using BMI2 instructions
6736  * carry:sum = sum + op1*op2 + carry
6737  * op2 should be in rdx
6738  * op2 is preserved, all other registers are modified
6739  */
6740 void MacroAssembler::multiply_add_64_bmi2(Register sum, Register op1, Register op2, Register carry, Register tmp2) {
6741   // assert op2 is rdx
6742   mulxq(tmp2, op1, op1);  //  op1 * op2 -> tmp2:op1
6743   addq(sum, carry);
6744   adcq(tmp2, 0);
6745   addq(sum, op1);
6746   adcq(tmp2, 0);
6747   movq(carry, tmp2);
6748 }
6749 
6750 /**
6751  * Perform the following multiply add operation:
6752  * carry:sum = sum + op1*op2 + carry
6753  * Preserves op1, op2 and modifies rest of registers
6754  */
6755 void MacroAssembler::multiply_add_64(Register sum, Register op1, Register op2, Register carry, Register rdxReg, Register raxReg) {
6756   // rdx:rax = op1 * op2
6757   movq(raxReg, op2);
6758   mulq(op1);
6759 
6760   //  rdx:rax = sum + carry + rdx:rax
6761   addq(sum, carry);
6762   adcq(rdxReg, 0);
6763   addq(sum, raxReg);
6764   adcq(rdxReg, 0);
6765 
6766   // carry:sum = rdx:sum
6767   movq(carry, rdxReg);
6768 }
6769 
6770 /**
6771  * Add 64 bit long carry into z[] with carry propogation.
6772  * Preserves z and carry register values and modifies rest of registers.
6773  *
6774  */
6775 void MacroAssembler::add_one_64(Register z, Register zlen, Register carry, Register tmp1) {
6776   Label L_fourth_loop, L_fourth_loop_exit;
6777 
6778   movl(tmp1, 1);
6779   subl(zlen, 2);
6780   addq(Address(z, zlen, Address::times_4, 0), carry);
6781 
6782   bind(L_fourth_loop);
6783   jccb(Assembler::carryClear, L_fourth_loop_exit);
6784   subl(zlen, 2);
6785   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_fourth_loop_exit);
6786   addq(Address(z, zlen, Address::times_4, 0), tmp1);
6787   jmp(L_fourth_loop);
6788   bind(L_fourth_loop_exit);
6789 }
6790 
6791 /**
6792  * Shift z[] left by 1 bit.
6793  * Preserves x, len, z and zlen registers and modifies rest of the registers.
6794  *
6795  */
6796 void MacroAssembler::lshift_by_1(Register x, Register len, Register z, Register zlen, Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3, Register tmp4) {
6797 
6798   Label L_fifth_loop, L_fifth_loop_exit;
6799 
6800   // Fifth loop
6801   // Perform primitiveLeftShift(z, zlen, 1)
6802 
6803   const Register prev_carry = tmp1;
6804   const Register new_carry = tmp4;
6805   const Register value = tmp2;
6806   const Register zidx = tmp3;
6807 
6808   // int zidx, carry;
6809   // long value;
6810   // carry = 0;
6811   // for (zidx = zlen-2; zidx >=0; zidx -= 2) {
6812   //    (carry:value)  = (z[i] << 1) | carry ;
6813   //    z[i] = value;
6814   // }
6815 
6816   movl(zidx, zlen);
6817   xorl(prev_carry, prev_carry); // clear carry flag and prev_carry register
6818 
6819   bind(L_fifth_loop);
6820   decl(zidx);  // Use decl to preserve carry flag
6821   decl(zidx);
6822   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_fifth_loop_exit);
6823 
6824   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
6825      movq(value, Address(z, zidx, Address::times_4, 0));
6826      rclq(value, 1);
6827      rorxq(value, value, 32);
6828      movq(Address(z, zidx, Address::times_4,  0), value);  // Store back in big endian form
6829   }
6830   else {
6831     // clear new_carry
6832     xorl(new_carry, new_carry);
6833 
6834     // Shift z[i] by 1, or in previous carry and save new carry
6835     movq(value, Address(z, zidx, Address::times_4, 0));
6836     shlq(value, 1);
6837     adcl(new_carry, 0);
6838 
6839     orq(value, prev_carry);
6840     rorq(value, 0x20);
6841     movq(Address(z, zidx, Address::times_4,  0), value);  // Store back in big endian form
6842 
6843     // Set previous carry = new carry
6844     movl(prev_carry, new_carry);
6845   }
6846   jmp(L_fifth_loop);
6847 
6848   bind(L_fifth_loop_exit);
6849 }
6850 
6851 
6852 /**
6853  * Code for BigInteger::squareToLen() intrinsic
6854  *
6855  * rdi: x
6856  * rsi: len
6857  * r8:  z
6858  * rcx: zlen
6859  * r12: tmp1
6860  * r13: tmp2
6861  * r14: tmp3
6862  * r15: tmp4
6863  * rbx: tmp5
6864  *
6865  */
6866 void MacroAssembler::square_to_len(Register x, Register len, Register z, Register zlen, Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3, Register tmp4, Register tmp5, Register rdxReg, Register raxReg) {
6867 
6868   Label L_second_loop, L_second_loop_exit, L_third_loop, L_third_loop_exit, L_last_x, L_multiply;
6869   push(tmp1);
6870   push(tmp2);
6871   push(tmp3);
6872   push(tmp4);
6873   push(tmp5);
6874 
6875   // First loop
6876   // Store the squares, right shifted one bit (i.e., divided by 2).
6877   square_rshift(x, len, z, tmp1, tmp3, tmp4, tmp5, rdxReg, raxReg);
6878 
6879   // Add in off-diagonal sums.
6880   //
6881   // Second, third (nested) and fourth loops.
6882   // zlen +=2;
6883   // for (int xidx=len-2,zidx=zlen-4; xidx > 0; xidx-=2,zidx-=4) {
6884   //    carry = 0;
6885   //    long op2 = x[xidx:xidx+1];
6886   //    for (int j=xidx-2,k=zidx; j >= 0; j-=2) {
6887   //       k -= 2;
6888   //       long op1 = x[j:j+1];
6889   //       long sum = z[k:k+1];
6890   //       carry:sum = multiply_add_64(sum, op1, op2, carry, tmp_regs);
6891   //       z[k:k+1] = sum;
6892   //    }
6893   //    add_one_64(z, k, carry, tmp_regs);
6894   // }
6895 
6896   const Register carry = tmp5;
6897   const Register sum = tmp3;
6898   const Register op1 = tmp4;
6899   Register op2 = tmp2;
6900 
6901   push(zlen);
6902   push(len);
6903   addl(zlen,2);
6904   bind(L_second_loop);
6905   xorq(carry, carry);
6906   subl(zlen, 4);
6907   subl(len, 2);
6908   push(zlen);
6909   push(len);
6910   cmpl(len, 0);
6911   jccb(Assembler::lessEqual, L_second_loop_exit);
6912 
6913   // Multiply an array by one 64 bit long.
6914   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
6915     op2 = rdxReg;
6916     movq(op2, Address(x, len, Address::times_4,  0));
6917     rorxq(op2, op2, 32);
6918   }
6919   else {
6920     movq(op2, Address(x, len, Address::times_4,  0));
6921     rorq(op2, 32);
6922   }
6923 
6924   bind(L_third_loop);
6925   decrementl(len);
6926   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_third_loop_exit);
6927   decrementl(len);
6928   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_last_x);
6929 
6930   movq(op1, Address(x, len, Address::times_4,  0));
6931   rorq(op1, 32);
6932 
6933   bind(L_multiply);
6934   subl(zlen, 2);
6935   movq(sum, Address(z, zlen, Address::times_4,  0));
6936 
6937   // Multiply 64 bit by 64 bit and add 64 bits lower half and upper 64 bits as carry.
6938   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
6939     multiply_add_64_bmi2(sum, op1, op2, carry, tmp2);
6940   }
6941   else {
6942     multiply_add_64(sum, op1, op2, carry, rdxReg, raxReg);
6943   }
6944 
6945   movq(Address(z, zlen, Address::times_4, 0), sum);
6946 
6947   jmp(L_third_loop);
6948   bind(L_third_loop_exit);
6949 
6950   // Fourth loop
6951   // Add 64 bit long carry into z with carry propogation.
6952   // Uses offsetted zlen.
6953   add_one_64(z, zlen, carry, tmp1);
6954 
6955   pop(len);
6956   pop(zlen);
6957   jmp(L_second_loop);
6958 
6959   // Next infrequent code is moved outside loops.
6960   bind(L_last_x);
6961   movl(op1, Address(x, 0));
6962   jmp(L_multiply);
6963 
6964   bind(L_second_loop_exit);
6965   pop(len);
6966   pop(zlen);
6967   pop(len);
6968   pop(zlen);
6969 
6970   // Fifth loop
6971   // Shift z left 1 bit.
6972   lshift_by_1(x, len, z, zlen, tmp1, tmp2, tmp3, tmp4);
6973 
6974   // z[zlen-1] |= x[len-1] & 1;
6975   movl(tmp3, Address(x, len, Address::times_4, -4));
6976   andl(tmp3, 1);
6977   orl(Address(z, zlen, Address::times_4,  -4), tmp3);
6978 
6979   pop(tmp5);
6980   pop(tmp4);
6981   pop(tmp3);
6982   pop(tmp2);
6983   pop(tmp1);
6984 }
6985 
6986 /**
6987  * Helper function for mul_add()
6988  * Multiply the in[] by int k and add to out[] starting at offset offs using
6989  * 128 bit by 32 bit multiply and return the carry in tmp5.
6990  * Only quad int aligned length of in[] is operated on in this function.
6991  * k is in rdxReg for BMI2Instructions, for others it is in tmp2.
6992  * This function preserves out, in and k registers.
6993  * len and offset point to the appropriate index in "in" & "out" correspondingly
6994  * tmp5 has the carry.
6995  * other registers are temporary and are modified.
6996  *
6997  */
6998 void MacroAssembler::mul_add_128_x_32_loop(Register out, Register in,
6999   Register offset, Register len, Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3,
7000   Register tmp4, Register tmp5, Register rdxReg, Register raxReg) {
7001 
7002   Label L_first_loop, L_first_loop_exit;
7003 
7004   movl(tmp1, len);
7005   shrl(tmp1, 2);
7006 
7007   bind(L_first_loop);
7008   subl(tmp1, 1);
7009   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_first_loop_exit);
7010 
7011   subl(len, 4);
7012   subl(offset, 4);
7013 
7014   Register op2 = tmp2;
7015   const Register sum = tmp3;
7016   const Register op1 = tmp4;
7017   const Register carry = tmp5;
7018 
7019   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
7020     op2 = rdxReg;
7021   }
7022 
7023   movq(op1, Address(in, len, Address::times_4,  8));
7024   rorq(op1, 32);
7025   movq(sum, Address(out, offset, Address::times_4,  8));
7026   rorq(sum, 32);
7027   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
7028     multiply_add_64_bmi2(sum, op1, op2, carry, raxReg);
7029   }
7030   else {
7031     multiply_add_64(sum, op1, op2, carry, rdxReg, raxReg);
7032   }
7033   // Store back in big endian from little endian
7034   rorq(sum, 0x20);
7035   movq(Address(out, offset, Address::times_4,  8), sum);
7036 
7037   movq(op1, Address(in, len, Address::times_4,  0));
7038   rorq(op1, 32);
7039   movq(sum, Address(out, offset, Address::times_4,  0));
7040   rorq(sum, 32);
7041   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
7042     multiply_add_64_bmi2(sum, op1, op2, carry, raxReg);
7043   }
7044   else {
7045     multiply_add_64(sum, op1, op2, carry, rdxReg, raxReg);
7046   }
7047   // Store back in big endian from little endian
7048   rorq(sum, 0x20);
7049   movq(Address(out, offset, Address::times_4,  0), sum);
7050 
7051   jmp(L_first_loop);
7052   bind(L_first_loop_exit);
7053 }
7054 
7055 /**
7056  * Code for BigInteger::mulAdd() intrinsic
7057  *
7058  * rdi: out
7059  * rsi: in
7060  * r11: offs (out.length - offset)
7061  * rcx: len
7062  * r8:  k
7063  * r12: tmp1
7064  * r13: tmp2
7065  * r14: tmp3
7066  * r15: tmp4
7067  * rbx: tmp5
7068  * Multiply the in[] by word k and add to out[], return the carry in rax
7069  */
7070 void MacroAssembler::mul_add(Register out, Register in, Register offs,
7071    Register len, Register k, Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3,
7072    Register tmp4, Register tmp5, Register rdxReg, Register raxReg) {
7073 
7074   Label L_carry, L_last_in, L_done;
7075 
7076 // carry = 0;
7077 // for (int j=len-1; j >= 0; j--) {
7078 //    long product = (in[j] & LONG_MASK) * kLong +
7079 //                   (out[offs] & LONG_MASK) + carry;
7080 //    out[offs--] = (int)product;
7081 //    carry = product >>> 32;
7082 // }
7083 //
7084   push(tmp1);
7085   push(tmp2);
7086   push(tmp3);
7087   push(tmp4);
7088   push(tmp5);
7089 
7090   Register op2 = tmp2;
7091   const Register sum = tmp3;
7092   const Register op1 = tmp4;
7093   const Register carry =  tmp5;
7094 
7095   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
7096     op2 = rdxReg;
7097     movl(op2, k);
7098   }
7099   else {
7100     movl(op2, k);
7101   }
7102 
7103   xorq(carry, carry);
7104 
7105   //First loop
7106 
7107   //Multiply in[] by k in a 4 way unrolled loop using 128 bit by 32 bit multiply
7108   //The carry is in tmp5
7109   mul_add_128_x_32_loop(out, in, offs, len, tmp1, tmp2, tmp3, tmp4, tmp5, rdxReg, raxReg);
7110 
7111   //Multiply the trailing in[] entry using 64 bit by 32 bit, if any
7112   decrementl(len);
7113   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_carry);
7114   decrementl(len);
7115   jccb(Assembler::negative, L_last_in);
7116 
7117   movq(op1, Address(in, len, Address::times_4,  0));
7118   rorq(op1, 32);
7119 
7120   subl(offs, 2);
7121   movq(sum, Address(out, offs, Address::times_4,  0));
7122   rorq(sum, 32);
7123 
7124   if (UseBMI2Instructions) {
7125     multiply_add_64_bmi2(sum, op1, op2, carry, raxReg);
7126   }
7127   else {
7128     multiply_add_64(sum, op1, op2, carry, rdxReg, raxReg);
7129   }
7130 
7131   // Store back in big endian from little endian
7132   rorq(sum, 0x20);
7133   movq(Address(out, offs, Address::times_4,  0), sum);
7134 
7135   testl(len, len);
7136   jccb(Assembler::zero, L_carry);
7137 
7138   //Multiply the last in[] entry, if any
7139   bind(L_last_in);
7140   movl(op1, Address(in, 0));
7141   movl(sum, Address(out, offs, Address::times_4,  -4));
7142 
7143   movl(raxReg, k);
7144   mull(op1); //tmp4 * eax -> edx:eax
7145   addl(sum, carry);
7146   adcl(rdxReg, 0);
7147   addl(sum, raxReg);
7148   adcl(rdxReg, 0);
7149   movl(carry, rdxReg);
7150 
7151   movl(Address(out, offs, Address::times_4,  -4), sum);
7152 
7153   bind(L_carry);
7154   //return tmp5/carry as carry in rax
7155   movl(rax, carry);
7156 
7157   bind(L_done);
7158   pop(tmp5);
7159   pop(tmp4);
7160   pop(tmp3);
7161   pop(tmp2);
7162   pop(tmp1);
7163 }
7164 #endif
7165 
7166 /**
7167  * Emits code to update CRC-32 with a byte value according to constants in table
7168  *
7169  * @param [in,out]crc   Register containing the crc.
7170  * @param [in]val       Register containing the byte to fold into the CRC.
7171  * @param [in]table     Register containing the table of crc constants.
7172  *
7173  * uint32_t crc;
7174  * val = crc_table[(val ^ crc) & 0xFF];
7175  * crc = val ^ (crc >> 8);
7176  *
7177  */
7178 void MacroAssembler::update_byte_crc32(Register crc, Register val, Register table) {
7179   xorl(val, crc);
7180   andl(val, 0xFF);
7181   shrl(crc, 8); // unsigned shift
7182   xorl(crc, Address(table, val, Address::times_4, 0));
7183 }
7184 
7185 /**
7186 * Fold four 128-bit data chunks
7187 */
7188 void MacroAssembler::fold_128bit_crc32_avx512(XMMRegister xcrc, XMMRegister xK, XMMRegister xtmp, Register buf, int offset) {
7189   evpclmulhdq(xtmp, xK, xcrc, Assembler::AVX_512bit); // [123:64]
7190   evpclmulldq(xcrc, xK, xcrc, Assembler::AVX_512bit); // [63:0]
7191   evpxorq(xcrc, xcrc, Address(buf, offset), Assembler::AVX_512bit /* vector_len */);
7192   evpxorq(xcrc, xcrc, xtmp, Assembler::AVX_512bit /* vector_len */);
7193 }
7194 
7195 /**
7196  * Fold 128-bit data chunk
7197  */
7198 void MacroAssembler::fold_128bit_crc32(XMMRegister xcrc, XMMRegister xK, XMMRegister xtmp, Register buf, int offset) {
7199   if (UseAVX > 0) {
7200     vpclmulhdq(xtmp, xK, xcrc); // [123:64]
7201     vpclmulldq(xcrc, xK, xcrc); // [63:0]
7202     vpxor(xcrc, xcrc, Address(buf, offset), 0 /* vector_len */);
7203     pxor(xcrc, xtmp);
7204   } else {
7205     movdqa(xtmp, xcrc);
7206     pclmulhdq(xtmp, xK);   // [123:64]
7207     pclmulldq(xcrc, xK);   // [63:0]
7208     pxor(xcrc, xtmp);
7209     movdqu(xtmp, Address(buf, offset));
7210     pxor(xcrc, xtmp);
7211   }
7212 }
7213 
7214 void MacroAssembler::fold_128bit_crc32(XMMRegister xcrc, XMMRegister xK, XMMRegister xtmp, XMMRegister xbuf) {
7215   if (UseAVX > 0) {
7216     vpclmulhdq(xtmp, xK, xcrc);
7217     vpclmulldq(xcrc, xK, xcrc);
7218     pxor(xcrc, xbuf);
7219     pxor(xcrc, xtmp);
7220   } else {
7221     movdqa(xtmp, xcrc);
7222     pclmulhdq(xtmp, xK);
7223     pclmulldq(xcrc, xK);
7224     pxor(xcrc, xbuf);
7225     pxor(xcrc, xtmp);
7226   }
7227 }
7228 
7229 /**
7230  * 8-bit folds to compute 32-bit CRC
7231  *
7232  * uint64_t xcrc;
7233  * timesXtoThe32[xcrc & 0xFF] ^ (xcrc >> 8);
7234  */
7235 void MacroAssembler::fold_8bit_crc32(XMMRegister xcrc, Register table, XMMRegister xtmp, Register tmp) {
7236   movdl(tmp, xcrc);
7237   andl(tmp, 0xFF);
7238   movdl(xtmp, Address(table, tmp, Address::times_4, 0));
7239   psrldq(xcrc, 1); // unsigned shift one byte
7240   pxor(xcrc, xtmp);
7241 }
7242 
7243 /**
7244  * uint32_t crc;
7245  * timesXtoThe32[crc & 0xFF] ^ (crc >> 8);
7246  */
7247 void MacroAssembler::fold_8bit_crc32(Register crc, Register table, Register tmp) {
7248   movl(tmp, crc);
7249   andl(tmp, 0xFF);
7250   shrl(crc, 8);
7251   xorl(crc, Address(table, tmp, Address::times_4, 0));
7252 }
7253 
7254 /**
7255  * @param crc   register containing existing CRC (32-bit)
7256  * @param buf   register pointing to input byte buffer (byte*)
7257  * @param len   register containing number of bytes
7258  * @param table register that will contain address of CRC table
7259  * @param tmp   scratch register
7260  */
7261 void MacroAssembler::kernel_crc32(Register crc, Register buf, Register len, Register table, Register tmp) {
7262   assert_different_registers(crc, buf, len, table, tmp, rax);
7263 
7264   Label L_tail, L_tail_restore, L_tail_loop, L_exit, L_align_loop, L_aligned;
7265   Label L_fold_tail, L_fold_128b, L_fold_512b, L_fold_512b_loop, L_fold_tail_loop;
7266 
7267   // For EVEX with VL and BW, provide a standard mask, VL = 128 will guide the merge
7268   // context for the registers used, where all instructions below are using 128-bit mode
7269   // On EVEX without VL and BW, these instructions will all be AVX.
7270   lea(table, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::crc_table_addr()));
7271   notl(crc); // ~crc
7272   cmpl(len, 16);
7273   jcc(Assembler::less, L_tail);
7274 
7275   // Align buffer to 16 bytes
7276   movl(tmp, buf);
7277   andl(tmp, 0xF);
7278   jccb(Assembler::zero, L_aligned);
7279   subl(tmp,  16);
7280   addl(len, tmp);
7281 
7282   align(4);
7283   BIND(L_align_loop);
7284   movsbl(rax, Address(buf, 0)); // load byte with sign extension
7285   update_byte_crc32(crc, rax, table);
7286   increment(buf);
7287   incrementl(tmp);
7288   jccb(Assembler::less, L_align_loop);
7289 
7290   BIND(L_aligned);
7291   movl(tmp, len); // save
7292   shrl(len, 4);
7293   jcc(Assembler::zero, L_tail_restore);
7294 
7295   // Fold crc into first bytes of vector
7296   movdqa(xmm1, Address(buf, 0));
7297   movdl(rax, xmm1);
7298   xorl(crc, rax);
7299   if (VM_Version::supports_sse4_1()) {
7300     pinsrd(xmm1, crc, 0);
7301   } else {
7302     pinsrw(xmm1, crc, 0);
7303     shrl(crc, 16);
7304     pinsrw(xmm1, crc, 1);
7305   }
7306   addptr(buf, 16);
7307   subl(len, 4); // len > 0
7308   jcc(Assembler::less, L_fold_tail);
7309 
7310   movdqa(xmm2, Address(buf,  0));
7311   movdqa(xmm3, Address(buf, 16));
7312   movdqa(xmm4, Address(buf, 32));
7313   addptr(buf, 48);
7314   subl(len, 3);
7315   jcc(Assembler::lessEqual, L_fold_512b);
7316 
7317   // Fold total 512 bits of polynomial on each iteration,
7318   // 128 bits per each of 4 parallel streams.
7319   movdqu(xmm0, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::x86::crc_by128_masks_addr() + 32));
7320 
7321   align(32);
7322   BIND(L_fold_512b_loop);
7323   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm1, xmm0, xmm5, buf,  0);
7324   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm2, xmm0, xmm5, buf, 16);
7325   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm3, xmm0, xmm5, buf, 32);
7326   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm4, xmm0, xmm5, buf, 48);
7327   addptr(buf, 64);
7328   subl(len, 4);
7329   jcc(Assembler::greater, L_fold_512b_loop);
7330 
7331   // Fold 512 bits to 128 bits.
7332   BIND(L_fold_512b);
7333   movdqu(xmm0, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::x86::crc_by128_masks_addr() + 16));
7334   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm1, xmm0, xmm5, xmm2);
7335   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm1, xmm0, xmm5, xmm3);
7336   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm1, xmm0, xmm5, xmm4);
7337 
7338   // Fold the rest of 128 bits data chunks
7339   BIND(L_fold_tail);
7340   addl(len, 3);
7341   jccb(Assembler::lessEqual, L_fold_128b);
7342   movdqu(xmm0, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::x86::crc_by128_masks_addr() + 16));
7343 
7344   BIND(L_fold_tail_loop);
7345   fold_128bit_crc32(xmm1, xmm0, xmm5, buf,  0);
7346   addptr(buf, 16);
7347   decrementl(len);
7348   jccb(Assembler::greater, L_fold_tail_loop);
7349 
7350   // Fold 128 bits in xmm1 down into 32 bits in crc register.
7351   BIND(L_fold_128b);
7352   movdqu(xmm0, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::x86::crc_by128_masks_addr()));
7353   if (UseAVX > 0) {
7354     vpclmulqdq(xmm2, xmm0, xmm1, 0x1);
7355     vpand(xmm3, xmm0, xmm2, 0 /* vector_len */);
7356     vpclmulqdq(xmm0, xmm0, xmm3, 0x1);
7357   } else {
7358     movdqa(xmm2, xmm0);
7359     pclmulqdq(xmm2, xmm1, 0x1);
7360     movdqa(xmm3, xmm0);
7361     pand(xmm3, xmm2);
7362     pclmulqdq(xmm0, xmm3, 0x1);
7363   }
7364   psrldq(xmm1, 8);
7365   psrldq(xmm2, 4);
7366   pxor(xmm0, xmm1);
7367   pxor(xmm0, xmm2);
7368 
7369   // 8 8-bit folds to compute 32-bit CRC.
7370   for (int j = 0; j < 4; j++) {
7371     fold_8bit_crc32(xmm0, table, xmm1, rax);
7372   }
7373   movdl(crc, xmm0); // mov 32 bits to general register
7374   for (int j = 0; j < 4; j++) {
7375     fold_8bit_crc32(crc, table, rax);
7376   }
7377 
7378   BIND(L_tail_restore);
7379   movl(len, tmp); // restore
7380   BIND(L_tail);
7381   andl(len, 0xf);
7382   jccb(Assembler::zero, L_exit);
7383 
7384   // Fold the rest of bytes
7385   align(4);
7386   BIND(L_tail_loop);
7387   movsbl(rax, Address(buf, 0)); // load byte with sign extension
7388   update_byte_crc32(crc, rax, table);
7389   increment(buf);
7390   decrementl(len);
7391   jccb(Assembler::greater, L_tail_loop);
7392 
7393   BIND(L_exit);
7394   notl(crc); // ~c
7395 }
7396 
7397 #ifdef _LP64
7398 // S. Gueron / Information Processing Letters 112 (2012) 184
7399 // Algorithm 4: Computing carry-less multiplication using a precomputed lookup table.
7400 // Input: A 32 bit value B = [byte3, byte2, byte1, byte0].
7401 // Output: the 64-bit carry-less product of B * CONST
7402 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_ipl_alg4(Register in, uint32_t n,
7403                                      Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3) {
7404   lea(tmp3, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::crc32c_table_addr()));
7405   if (n > 0) {
7406     addq(tmp3, n * 256 * 8);
7407   }
7408   //    Q1 = TABLEExt[n][B & 0xFF];
7409   movl(tmp1, in);
7410   andl(tmp1, 0x000000FF);
7411   shll(tmp1, 3);
7412   addq(tmp1, tmp3);
7413   movq(tmp1, Address(tmp1, 0));
7414 
7415   //    Q2 = TABLEExt[n][B >> 8 & 0xFF];
7416   movl(tmp2, in);
7417   shrl(tmp2, 8);
7418   andl(tmp2, 0x000000FF);
7419   shll(tmp2, 3);
7420   addq(tmp2, tmp3);
7421   movq(tmp2, Address(tmp2, 0));
7422 
7423   shlq(tmp2, 8);
7424   xorq(tmp1, tmp2);
7425 
7426   //    Q3 = TABLEExt[n][B >> 16 & 0xFF];
7427   movl(tmp2, in);
7428   shrl(tmp2, 16);
7429   andl(tmp2, 0x000000FF);
7430   shll(tmp2, 3);
7431   addq(tmp2, tmp3);
7432   movq(tmp2, Address(tmp2, 0));
7433 
7434   shlq(tmp2, 16);
7435   xorq(tmp1, tmp2);
7436 
7437   //    Q4 = TABLEExt[n][B >> 24 & 0xFF];
7438   shrl(in, 24);
7439   andl(in, 0x000000FF);
7440   shll(in, 3);
7441   addq(in, tmp3);
7442   movq(in, Address(in, 0));
7443 
7444   shlq(in, 24);
7445   xorq(in, tmp1);
7446   //    return Q1 ^ Q2 << 8 ^ Q3 << 16 ^ Q4 << 24;
7447 }
7448 
7449 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_pclmulqdq(XMMRegister w_xtmp1,
7450                                       Register in_out,
7451                                       uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index, bool is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7452                                       XMMRegister w_xtmp2,
7453                                       Register tmp1,
7454                                       Register n_tmp2, Register n_tmp3) {
7455   if (is_pclmulqdq_supported) {
7456     movdl(w_xtmp1, in_out); // modified blindly
7457 
7458     movl(tmp1, const_or_pre_comp_const_index);
7459     movdl(w_xtmp2, tmp1);
7460     pclmulqdq(w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, 0);
7461 
7462     movdq(in_out, w_xtmp1);
7463   } else {
7464     crc32c_ipl_alg4(in_out, const_or_pre_comp_const_index, tmp1, n_tmp2, n_tmp3);
7465   }
7466 }
7467 
7468 // Recombination Alternative 2: No bit-reflections
7469 // T1 = (CRC_A * U1) << 1
7470 // T2 = (CRC_B * U2) << 1
7471 // C1 = T1 >> 32
7472 // C2 = T2 >> 32
7473 // T1 = T1 & 0xFFFFFFFF
7474 // T2 = T2 & 0xFFFFFFFF
7475 // T1 = CRC32(0, T1)
7476 // T2 = CRC32(0, T2)
7477 // C1 = C1 ^ T1
7478 // C2 = C2 ^ T2
7479 // CRC = C1 ^ C2 ^ CRC_C
7480 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_rec_alt2(uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, bool is_pclmulqdq_supported, Register in_out, Register in1, Register in2,
7481                                      XMMRegister w_xtmp1, XMMRegister w_xtmp2, XMMRegister w_xtmp3,
7482                                      Register tmp1, Register tmp2,
7483                                      Register n_tmp3) {
7484   crc32c_pclmulqdq(w_xtmp1, in_out, const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, is_pclmulqdq_supported, w_xtmp3, tmp1, tmp2, n_tmp3);
7485   crc32c_pclmulqdq(w_xtmp2, in1, const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, is_pclmulqdq_supported, w_xtmp3, tmp1, tmp2, n_tmp3);
7486   shlq(in_out, 1);
7487   movl(tmp1, in_out);
7488   shrq(in_out, 32);
7489   xorl(tmp2, tmp2);
7490   crc32(tmp2, tmp1, 4);
7491   xorl(in_out, tmp2); // we don't care about upper 32 bit contents here
7492   shlq(in1, 1);
7493   movl(tmp1, in1);
7494   shrq(in1, 32);
7495   xorl(tmp2, tmp2);
7496   crc32(tmp2, tmp1, 4);
7497   xorl(in1, tmp2);
7498   xorl(in_out, in1);
7499   xorl(in_out, in2);
7500 }
7501 
7502 // Set N to predefined value
7503 // Subtract from a lenght of a buffer
7504 // execute in a loop:
7505 // CRC_A = 0xFFFFFFFF, CRC_B = 0, CRC_C = 0
7506 // for i = 1 to N do
7507 //  CRC_A = CRC32(CRC_A, A[i])
7508 //  CRC_B = CRC32(CRC_B, B[i])
7509 //  CRC_C = CRC32(CRC_C, C[i])
7510 // end for
7511 // Recombine
7512 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_proc_chunk(uint32_t size, uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, bool is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7513                                        Register in_out1, Register in_out2, Register in_out3,
7514                                        Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3,
7515                                        XMMRegister w_xtmp1, XMMRegister w_xtmp2, XMMRegister w_xtmp3,
7516                                        Register tmp4, Register tmp5,
7517                                        Register n_tmp6) {
7518   Label L_processPartitions;
7519   Label L_processPartition;
7520   Label L_exit;
7521 
7522   bind(L_processPartitions);
7523   cmpl(in_out1, 3 * size);
7524   jcc(Assembler::less, L_exit);
7525     xorl(tmp1, tmp1);
7526     xorl(tmp2, tmp2);
7527     movq(tmp3, in_out2);
7528     addq(tmp3, size);
7529 
7530     bind(L_processPartition);
7531       crc32(in_out3, Address(in_out2, 0), 8);
7532       crc32(tmp1, Address(in_out2, size), 8);
7533       crc32(tmp2, Address(in_out2, size * 2), 8);
7534       addq(in_out2, 8);
7535       cmpq(in_out2, tmp3);
7536       jcc(Assembler::less, L_processPartition);
7537     crc32c_rec_alt2(const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, is_pclmulqdq_supported, in_out3, tmp1, tmp2,
7538             w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7539             tmp4, tmp5,
7540             n_tmp6);
7541     addq(in_out2, 2 * size);
7542     subl(in_out1, 3 * size);
7543     jmp(L_processPartitions);
7544 
7545   bind(L_exit);
7546 }
7547 #else
7548 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_ipl_alg4(Register in_out, uint32_t n,
7549                                      Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3,
7550                                      XMMRegister xtmp1, XMMRegister xtmp2) {
7551   lea(tmp3, ExternalAddress(StubRoutines::crc32c_table_addr()));
7552   if (n > 0) {
7553     addl(tmp3, n * 256 * 8);
7554   }
7555   //    Q1 = TABLEExt[n][B & 0xFF];
7556   movl(tmp1, in_out);
7557   andl(tmp1, 0x000000FF);
7558   shll(tmp1, 3);
7559   addl(tmp1, tmp3);
7560   movq(xtmp1, Address(tmp1, 0));
7561 
7562   //    Q2 = TABLEExt[n][B >> 8 & 0xFF];
7563   movl(tmp2, in_out);
7564   shrl(tmp2, 8);
7565   andl(tmp2, 0x000000FF);
7566   shll(tmp2, 3);
7567   addl(tmp2, tmp3);
7568   movq(xtmp2, Address(tmp2, 0));
7569 
7570   psllq(xtmp2, 8);
7571   pxor(xtmp1, xtmp2);
7572 
7573   //    Q3 = TABLEExt[n][B >> 16 & 0xFF];
7574   movl(tmp2, in_out);
7575   shrl(tmp2, 16);
7576   andl(tmp2, 0x000000FF);
7577   shll(tmp2, 3);
7578   addl(tmp2, tmp3);
7579   movq(xtmp2, Address(tmp2, 0));
7580 
7581   psllq(xtmp2, 16);
7582   pxor(xtmp1, xtmp2);
7583 
7584   //    Q4 = TABLEExt[n][B >> 24 & 0xFF];
7585   shrl(in_out, 24);
7586   andl(in_out, 0x000000FF);
7587   shll(in_out, 3);
7588   addl(in_out, tmp3);
7589   movq(xtmp2, Address(in_out, 0));
7590 
7591   psllq(xtmp2, 24);
7592   pxor(xtmp1, xtmp2); // Result in CXMM
7593   //    return Q1 ^ Q2 << 8 ^ Q3 << 16 ^ Q4 << 24;
7594 }
7595 
7596 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_pclmulqdq(XMMRegister w_xtmp1,
7597                                       Register in_out,
7598                                       uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index, bool is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7599                                       XMMRegister w_xtmp2,
7600                                       Register tmp1,
7601                                       Register n_tmp2, Register n_tmp3) {
7602   if (is_pclmulqdq_supported) {
7603     movdl(w_xtmp1, in_out);
7604 
7605     movl(tmp1, const_or_pre_comp_const_index);
7606     movdl(w_xtmp2, tmp1);
7607     pclmulqdq(w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, 0);
7608     // Keep result in XMM since GPR is 32 bit in length
7609   } else {
7610     crc32c_ipl_alg4(in_out, const_or_pre_comp_const_index, tmp1, n_tmp2, n_tmp3, w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2);
7611   }
7612 }
7613 
7614 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_rec_alt2(uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, bool is_pclmulqdq_supported, Register in_out, Register in1, Register in2,
7615                                      XMMRegister w_xtmp1, XMMRegister w_xtmp2, XMMRegister w_xtmp3,
7616                                      Register tmp1, Register tmp2,
7617                                      Register n_tmp3) {
7618   crc32c_pclmulqdq(w_xtmp1, in_out, const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, is_pclmulqdq_supported, w_xtmp3, tmp1, tmp2, n_tmp3);
7619   crc32c_pclmulqdq(w_xtmp2, in1, const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, is_pclmulqdq_supported, w_xtmp3, tmp1, tmp2, n_tmp3);
7620 
7621   psllq(w_xtmp1, 1);
7622   movdl(tmp1, w_xtmp1);
7623   psrlq(w_xtmp1, 32);
7624   movdl(in_out, w_xtmp1);
7625 
7626   xorl(tmp2, tmp2);
7627   crc32(tmp2, tmp1, 4);
7628   xorl(in_out, tmp2);
7629 
7630   psllq(w_xtmp2, 1);
7631   movdl(tmp1, w_xtmp2);
7632   psrlq(w_xtmp2, 32);
7633   movdl(in1, w_xtmp2);
7634 
7635   xorl(tmp2, tmp2);
7636   crc32(tmp2, tmp1, 4);
7637   xorl(in1, tmp2);
7638   xorl(in_out, in1);
7639   xorl(in_out, in2);
7640 }
7641 
7642 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_proc_chunk(uint32_t size, uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, bool is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7643                                        Register in_out1, Register in_out2, Register in_out3,
7644                                        Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3,
7645                                        XMMRegister w_xtmp1, XMMRegister w_xtmp2, XMMRegister w_xtmp3,
7646                                        Register tmp4, Register tmp5,
7647                                        Register n_tmp6) {
7648   Label L_processPartitions;
7649   Label L_processPartition;
7650   Label L_exit;
7651 
7652   bind(L_processPartitions);
7653   cmpl(in_out1, 3 * size);
7654   jcc(Assembler::less, L_exit);
7655     xorl(tmp1, tmp1);
7656     xorl(tmp2, tmp2);
7657     movl(tmp3, in_out2);
7658     addl(tmp3, size);
7659 
7660     bind(L_processPartition);
7661       crc32(in_out3, Address(in_out2, 0), 4);
7662       crc32(tmp1, Address(in_out2, size), 4);
7663       crc32(tmp2, Address(in_out2, size*2), 4);
7664       crc32(in_out3, Address(in_out2, 0+4), 4);
7665       crc32(tmp1, Address(in_out2, size+4), 4);
7666       crc32(tmp2, Address(in_out2, size*2+4), 4);
7667       addl(in_out2, 8);
7668       cmpl(in_out2, tmp3);
7669       jcc(Assembler::less, L_processPartition);
7670 
7671         push(tmp3);
7672         push(in_out1);
7673         push(in_out2);
7674         tmp4 = tmp3;
7675         tmp5 = in_out1;
7676         n_tmp6 = in_out2;
7677 
7678       crc32c_rec_alt2(const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u1, const_or_pre_comp_const_index_u2, is_pclmulqdq_supported, in_out3, tmp1, tmp2,
7679             w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7680             tmp4, tmp5,
7681             n_tmp6);
7682 
7683         pop(in_out2);
7684         pop(in_out1);
7685         pop(tmp3);
7686 
7687     addl(in_out2, 2 * size);
7688     subl(in_out1, 3 * size);
7689     jmp(L_processPartitions);
7690 
7691   bind(L_exit);
7692 }
7693 #endif //LP64
7694 
7695 #ifdef _LP64
7696 // Algorithm 2: Pipelined usage of the CRC32 instruction.
7697 // Input: A buffer I of L bytes.
7698 // Output: the CRC32C value of the buffer.
7699 // Notations:
7700 // Write L = 24N + r, with N = floor (L/24).
7701 // r = L mod 24 (0 <= r < 24).
7702 // Consider I as the concatenation of A|B|C|R, where A, B, C, each,
7703 // N quadwords, and R consists of r bytes.
7704 // A[j] = I [8j+7:8j], j= 0, 1, ..., N-1
7705 // B[j] = I [N + 8j+7:N + 8j], j= 0, 1, ..., N-1
7706 // C[j] = I [2N + 8j+7:2N + 8j], j= 0, 1, ..., N-1
7707 // if r > 0 R[j] = I [3N +j], j= 0, 1, ...,r-1
7708 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_ipl_alg2_alt2(Register in_out, Register in1, Register in2,
7709                                           Register tmp1, Register tmp2, Register tmp3,
7710                                           Register tmp4, Register tmp5, Register tmp6,
7711                                           XMMRegister w_xtmp1, XMMRegister w_xtmp2, XMMRegister w_xtmp3,
7712                                           bool is_pclmulqdq_supported) {
7713   uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index[CRC32C_NUM_PRECOMPUTED_CONSTANTS];
7714   Label L_wordByWord;
7715   Label L_byteByByteProlog;
7716   Label L_byteByByte;
7717   Label L_exit;
7718 
7719   if (is_pclmulqdq_supported ) {
7720     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[1] = *(uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr;
7721     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[0] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr+1);
7722 
7723     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[3] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 2);
7724     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[2] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 3);
7725 
7726     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[5] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 4);
7727     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[4] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 5);
7728     assert((CRC32C_NUM_PRECOMPUTED_CONSTANTS - 1 ) == 5, "Checking whether you declared all of the constants based on the number of \"chunks\"");
7729   } else {
7730     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[0] = 1;
7731     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[1] = 0;
7732 
7733     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[2] = 3;
7734     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[3] = 2;
7735 
7736     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[4] = 5;
7737     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[5] = 4;
7738    }
7739   crc32c_proc_chunk(CRC32C_HIGH, const_or_pre_comp_const_index[0], const_or_pre_comp_const_index[1], is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7740                     in2, in1, in_out,
7741                     tmp1, tmp2, tmp3,
7742                     w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7743                     tmp4, tmp5,
7744                     tmp6);
7745   crc32c_proc_chunk(CRC32C_MIDDLE, const_or_pre_comp_const_index[2], const_or_pre_comp_const_index[3], is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7746                     in2, in1, in_out,
7747                     tmp1, tmp2, tmp3,
7748                     w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7749                     tmp4, tmp5,
7750                     tmp6);
7751   crc32c_proc_chunk(CRC32C_LOW, const_or_pre_comp_const_index[4], const_or_pre_comp_const_index[5], is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7752                     in2, in1, in_out,
7753                     tmp1, tmp2, tmp3,
7754                     w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7755                     tmp4, tmp5,
7756                     tmp6);
7757   movl(tmp1, in2);
7758   andl(tmp1, 0x00000007);
7759   negl(tmp1);
7760   addl(tmp1, in2);
7761   addq(tmp1, in1);
7762 
7763   BIND(L_wordByWord);
7764   cmpq(in1, tmp1);
7765   jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_byteByByteProlog);
7766     crc32(in_out, Address(in1, 0), 4);
7767     addq(in1, 4);
7768     jmp(L_wordByWord);
7769 
7770   BIND(L_byteByByteProlog);
7771   andl(in2, 0x00000007);
7772   movl(tmp2, 1);
7773 
7774   BIND(L_byteByByte);
7775   cmpl(tmp2, in2);
7776   jccb(Assembler::greater, L_exit);
7777     crc32(in_out, Address(in1, 0), 1);
7778     incq(in1);
7779     incl(tmp2);
7780     jmp(L_byteByByte);
7781 
7782   BIND(L_exit);
7783 }
7784 #else
7785 void MacroAssembler::crc32c_ipl_alg2_alt2(Register in_out, Register in1, Register in2,
7786                                           Register tmp1, Register  tmp2, Register tmp3,
7787                                           Register tmp4, Register  tmp5, Register tmp6,
7788                                           XMMRegister w_xtmp1, XMMRegister w_xtmp2, XMMRegister w_xtmp3,
7789                                           bool is_pclmulqdq_supported) {
7790   uint32_t const_or_pre_comp_const_index[CRC32C_NUM_PRECOMPUTED_CONSTANTS];
7791   Label L_wordByWord;
7792   Label L_byteByByteProlog;
7793   Label L_byteByByte;
7794   Label L_exit;
7795 
7796   if (is_pclmulqdq_supported) {
7797     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[1] = *(uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr;
7798     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[0] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 1);
7799 
7800     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[3] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 2);
7801     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[2] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 3);
7802 
7803     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[5] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 4);
7804     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[4] = *((uint32_t *)StubRoutines::_crc32c_table_addr + 5);
7805   } else {
7806     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[0] = 1;
7807     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[1] = 0;
7808 
7809     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[2] = 3;
7810     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[3] = 2;
7811 
7812     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[4] = 5;
7813     const_or_pre_comp_const_index[5] = 4;
7814   }
7815   crc32c_proc_chunk(CRC32C_HIGH, const_or_pre_comp_const_index[0], const_or_pre_comp_const_index[1], is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7816                     in2, in1, in_out,
7817                     tmp1, tmp2, tmp3,
7818                     w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7819                     tmp4, tmp5,
7820                     tmp6);
7821   crc32c_proc_chunk(CRC32C_MIDDLE, const_or_pre_comp_const_index[2], const_or_pre_comp_const_index[3], is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7822                     in2, in1, in_out,
7823                     tmp1, tmp2, tmp3,
7824                     w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7825                     tmp4, tmp5,
7826                     tmp6);
7827   crc32c_proc_chunk(CRC32C_LOW, const_or_pre_comp_const_index[4], const_or_pre_comp_const_index[5], is_pclmulqdq_supported,
7828                     in2, in1, in_out,
7829                     tmp1, tmp2, tmp3,
7830                     w_xtmp1, w_xtmp2, w_xtmp3,
7831                     tmp4, tmp5,
7832                     tmp6);
7833   movl(tmp1, in2);
7834   andl(tmp1, 0x00000007);
7835   negl(tmp1);
7836   addl(tmp1, in2);
7837   addl(tmp1, in1);
7838 
7839   BIND(L_wordByWord);
7840   cmpl(in1, tmp1);
7841   jcc(Assembler::greaterEqual, L_byteByByteProlog);
7842     crc32(in_out, Address(in1,0), 4);
7843     addl(in1, 4);
7844     jmp(L_wordByWord);
7845 
7846   BIND(L_byteByByteProlog);
7847   andl(in2, 0x00000007);
7848   movl(tmp2, 1);
7849 
7850   BIND(L_byteByByte);
7851   cmpl(tmp2, in2);
7852   jccb(Assembler::greater, L_exit);
7853     movb(tmp1, Address(in1, 0));
7854     crc32(in_out, tmp1, 1);
7855     incl(in1);
7856     incl(tmp2);
7857     jmp(L_byteByByte);
7858 
7859   BIND(L_exit);
7860 }
7861 #endif // LP64
7862 #undef BIND
7863 #undef BLOCK_COMMENT
