7865 // Compress char[] array to byte[].
7866 //   ..\jdk\src\java.base\share\classes\java\lang\StringUTF16.java
7867 //   @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate
7868 //   private static int compress(char[] src, int srcOff, byte[] dst, int dstOff, int len) {
7869 //     for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
7870 //       int c = src[srcOff++];
7871 //       if (c >>> 8 != 0) {
7872 //         return 0;
7873 //       }
7874 //       dst[dstOff++] = (byte)c;
7875 //     }
7876 //     return len;
7877 //   }
7878 void MacroAssembler::char_array_compress(Register src, Register dst, Register len,
7879   XMMRegister tmp1Reg, XMMRegister tmp2Reg,
7880   XMMRegister tmp3Reg, XMMRegister tmp4Reg,
7881   Register tmp5, Register result) {
7882   Label copy_chars_loop, return_length, return_zero, done;
7883 
7884   // rsi: src
7885   // rdi: dst
7886   // rdx: len
7887   // rcx: tmp5
7888   // rax: result
7889 
7890   // rsi holds start addr of source char[] to be compressed
7891   // rdi holds start addr of destination byte[]
7892   // rdx holds length
7893 
7894   assert(len != result, "");
7895 
7896   // save length for return
7897   push(len);
7898 
7899   if ((AVX3Threshold == 0) && (UseAVX > 2) && // AVX512
7900     VM_Version::supports_avx512vlbw() &&
7901     VM_Version::supports_bmi2()) {
7902 
7903     Label copy_32_loop, copy_loop_tail, below_threshold;
7904 
7905     // alignment
7906     Label post_alignment;
7907 
7908     // if length of the string is less than 16, handle it in an old fashioned way
7909     testl(len, -32);
7910     jcc(Assembler::zero, below_threshold);
7911 
7912     // First check whether a character is compressable ( <= 0xFF).
7913     // Create mask to test for Unicode chars inside zmm vector
7914     movl(result, 0x00FF);
7915     evpbroadcastw(tmp2Reg, result, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7916 
7917     testl(len, -64);
7918     jcc(Assembler::zero, post_alignment);
7919 
7920     movl(tmp5, dst);
7921     andl(tmp5, (32 - 1));
7922     negl(tmp5);
7923     andl(tmp5, (32 - 1));
7924 
7925     // bail out when there is nothing to be done
7926     testl(tmp5, 0xFFFFFFFF);
7927     jcc(Assembler::zero, post_alignment);
7928 
7929     // ~(~0 << len), where len is the # of remaining elements to process
7930     movl(result, 0xFFFFFFFF);
7931     shlxl(result, result, tmp5);
7932     notl(result);
7933     kmovdl(k3, result);
7934 
7935     evmovdquw(tmp1Reg, k3, Address(src, 0), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7936     evpcmpuw(k2, k3, tmp1Reg, tmp2Reg, Assembler::le, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7937     ktestd(k2, k3);
7938     jcc(Assembler::carryClear, return_zero);
7939 
7940     evpmovwb(Address(dst, 0), k3, tmp1Reg, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7941 
7942     addptr(src, tmp5);
7943     addptr(src, tmp5);
7944     addptr(dst, tmp5);
7945     subl(len, tmp5);
7946 
7947     bind(post_alignment);
7948     // end of alignment
7949 
7950     movl(tmp5, len);
7951     andl(tmp5, (32 - 1));    // tail count (in chars)
7952     andl(len, ~(32 - 1));    // vector count (in chars)
7953     jcc(Assembler::zero, copy_loop_tail);
7954 
7955     lea(src, Address(src, len, Address::times_2));
7956     lea(dst, Address(dst, len, Address::times_1));
7957     negptr(len);
7958 
7959     bind(copy_32_loop);
7960     evmovdquw(tmp1Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7961     evpcmpuw(k2, tmp1Reg, tmp2Reg, Assembler::le, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7962     kortestdl(k2, k2);
7963     jcc(Assembler::carryClear, return_zero);
7964 
7965     // All elements in current processed chunk are valid candidates for
7966     // compression. Write a truncated byte elements to the memory.
7967     evpmovwb(Address(dst, len, Address::times_1), tmp1Reg, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7968     addptr(len, 32);
7969     jcc(Assembler::notZero, copy_32_loop);
7970 
7971     bind(copy_loop_tail);
7972     // bail out when there is nothing to be done
7973     testl(tmp5, 0xFFFFFFFF);
7974     jcc(Assembler::zero, return_length);
7975 
7976     movl(len, tmp5);
7977 
7978     // ~(~0 << len), where len is the # of remaining elements to process
7979     movl(result, 0xFFFFFFFF);
7980     shlxl(result, result, len);
7981     notl(result);
7982 
7983     kmovdl(k3, result);
7984 
7985     evmovdquw(tmp1Reg, k3, Address(src, 0), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7986     evpcmpuw(k2, k3, tmp1Reg, tmp2Reg, Assembler::le, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7987     ktestd(k2, k3);
7988     jcc(Assembler::carryClear, return_zero);
7989 
7990     evpmovwb(Address(dst, 0), k3, tmp1Reg, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
7991     jmp(return_length);
7992 
7993     bind(below_threshold);
7994   }
7995 
7996   if (UseSSE42Intrinsics) {
7997     Label copy_32_loop, copy_16, copy_tail;
7998 
7999     movl(result, len);
8000 
8001     movl(tmp5, 0xff00ff00);   // create mask to test for Unicode chars in vectors
8002 
8003     // vectored compression
8004     andl(len, 0xfffffff0);    // vector count (in chars)
8005     andl(result, 0x0000000f);    // tail count (in chars)
8006     testl(len, len);
8007     jcc(Assembler::zero, copy_16);
8008 
8009     // compress 16 chars per iter
8010     movdl(tmp1Reg, tmp5);
8011     pshufd(tmp1Reg, tmp1Reg, 0);   // store Unicode mask in tmp1Reg
8012     pxor(tmp4Reg, tmp4Reg);
8013 
8014     lea(src, Address(src, len, Address::times_2));
8015     lea(dst, Address(dst, len, Address::times_1));
8016     negptr(len);
8017 
8018     bind(copy_32_loop);
8019     movdqu(tmp2Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2));     // load 1st 8 characters
8020     por(tmp4Reg, tmp2Reg);
8021     movdqu(tmp3Reg, Address(src, len, Address::times_2, 16)); // load next 8 characters
8022     por(tmp4Reg, tmp3Reg);
8023     ptest(tmp4Reg, tmp1Reg);       // check for Unicode chars in next vector
8024     jcc(Assembler::notZero, return_zero);
8025     packuswb(tmp2Reg, tmp3Reg);    // only ASCII chars; compress each to 1 byte
8026     movdqu(Address(dst, len, Address::times_1), tmp2Reg);
8027     addptr(len, 16);
8028     jcc(Assembler::notZero, copy_32_loop);
8029 
8030     // compress next vector of 8 chars (if any)
8031     bind(copy_16);
8032     movl(len, result);
8033     andl(len, 0xfffffff8);    // vector count (in chars)
8034     andl(result, 0x00000007);    // tail count (in chars)
8035     testl(len, len);
8036     jccb(Assembler::zero, copy_tail);
8037 
8038     movdl(tmp1Reg, tmp5);
8039     pshufd(tmp1Reg, tmp1Reg, 0);   // store Unicode mask in tmp1Reg
8040     pxor(tmp3Reg, tmp3Reg);
8041 
8042     movdqu(tmp2Reg, Address(src, 0));
8043     ptest(tmp2Reg, tmp1Reg);       // check for Unicode chars in vector
8044     jccb(Assembler::notZero, return_zero);
8045     packuswb(tmp2Reg, tmp3Reg);    // only LATIN1 chars; compress each to 1 byte
8046     movq(Address(dst, 0), tmp2Reg);
8047     addptr(src, 16);
8048     addptr(dst, 8);
8049 
8050     bind(copy_tail);
8051     movl(len, result);
8052   }
8053   // compress 1 char per iter
8054   testl(len, len);
8055   jccb(Assembler::zero, return_length);
8056   lea(src, Address(src, len, Address::times_2));
8057   lea(dst, Address(dst, len, Address::times_1));
8058   negptr(len);
8059 
8060   bind(copy_chars_loop);
8061   load_unsigned_short(result, Address(src, len, Address::times_2));
8062   testl(result, 0xff00);      // check if Unicode char
8063   jccb(Assembler::notZero, return_zero);
8064   movb(Address(dst, len, Address::times_1), result);  // ASCII char; compress to 1 byte
8065   increment(len);
8066   jcc(Assembler::notZero, copy_chars_loop);
8067 
8068   // if compression succeeded, return length
8069   bind(return_length);
8070   pop(result);
8071   jmpb(done);
8072 
8073   // if compression failed, return 0
8074   bind(return_zero);
8075   xorl(result, result);
8076   addptr(rsp, wordSize);
8077 
8078   bind(done);
8079 }
8080 
8081 // Inflate byte[] array to char[].
8082 //   ..\jdk\src\java.base\share\classes\java\lang\StringLatin1.java
8083 //   @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate
8084 //   private static void inflate(byte[] src, int srcOff, char[] dst, int dstOff, int len) {
8085 //     for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
8086 //       dst[dstOff++] = (char)(src[srcOff++] & 0xff);
8087 //     }
8088 //   }
8089 void MacroAssembler::byte_array_inflate(Register src, Register dst, Register len,
8090   XMMRegister tmp1, Register tmp2) {
8091   Label copy_chars_loop, done, below_threshold, avx3_threshold;
8092   // rsi: src
8093   // rdi: dst
8094   // rdx: len
8095   // rcx: tmp2
8096 
8097   // rsi holds start addr of source byte[] to be inflated
8098   // rdi holds start addr of destination char[]
8099   // rdx holds length
8100   assert_different_registers(src, dst, len, tmp2);
8101   movl(tmp2, len);
8102   if ((UseAVX > 2) && // AVX512
8103     VM_Version::supports_avx512vlbw() &&
8104     VM_Version::supports_bmi2()) {
8105 
8106     Label copy_32_loop, copy_tail;
8107     Register tmp3_aliased = len;
8108 
8109     // if length of the string is less than 16, handle it in an old fashioned way
8110     testl(len, -16);
8111     jcc(Assembler::zero, below_threshold);
8112 
8113     testl(len, -1 * AVX3Threshold);
8114     jcc(Assembler::zero, avx3_threshold);
8115 
8116     // In order to use only one arithmetic operation for the main loop we use
8117     // this pre-calculation
8118     andl(tmp2, (32 - 1)); // tail count (in chars), 32 element wide loop
8119     andl(len, -32);     // vector count
8120     jccb(Assembler::zero, copy_tail);
8121 
8122     lea(src, Address(src, len, Address::times_1));
8123     lea(dst, Address(dst, len, Address::times_2));
8124     negptr(len);
8125 
8126 
8127     // inflate 32 chars per iter
8128     bind(copy_32_loop);
8129     vpmovzxbw(tmp1, Address(src, len, Address::times_1), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
8130     evmovdquw(Address(dst, len, Address::times_2), tmp1, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
8131     addptr(len, 32);
8132     jcc(Assembler::notZero, copy_32_loop);
8133 
8134     bind(copy_tail);
8135     // bail out when there is nothing to be done
8136     testl(tmp2, -1); // we don't destroy the contents of tmp2 here
8137     jcc(Assembler::zero, done);
8138 
8139     // ~(~0 << length), where length is the # of remaining elements to process
8140     movl(tmp3_aliased, -1);
8141     shlxl(tmp3_aliased, tmp3_aliased, tmp2);
8142     notl(tmp3_aliased);
8143     kmovdl(k2, tmp3_aliased);
8144     evpmovzxbw(tmp1, k2, Address(src, 0), Assembler::AVX_512bit);
8145     evmovdquw(Address(dst, 0), k2, tmp1, Assembler::AVX_512bit);
8146 
8147     jmp(done);
8148     bind(avx3_threshold);
8149   }
8150   if (UseSSE42Intrinsics) {
8151     Label copy_16_loop, copy_8_loop, copy_bytes, copy_new_tail, copy_tail;
8152 
8153     if (UseAVX > 1) {
8154       andl(tmp2, (16 - 1));
8155       andl(len, -16);
8156       jccb(Assembler::zero, copy_new_tail);
8157     } else {
8158       andl(tmp2, 0x00000007);   // tail count (in chars)
8159       andl(len, 0xfffffff8);    // vector count (in chars)
8160       jccb(Assembler::zero, copy_tail);
8161     }
8162 
8163     // vectored inflation
8164     lea(src, Address(src, len, Address::times_1));
8165     lea(dst, Address(dst, len, Address::times_2));
8166     negptr(len);
8167 
8168     if (UseAVX > 1) {
8169       bind(copy_16_loop);
8170       vpmovzxbw(tmp1, Address(src, len, Address::times_1), Assembler::AVX_256bit);
8171       vmovdqu(Address(dst, len, Address::times_2), tmp1);
8172       addptr(len, 16);
8173       jcc(Assembler::notZero, copy_16_loop);
8174 
8175       bind(below_threshold);
8176       bind(copy_new_tail);
8177       movl(len, tmp2);
8178       andl(tmp2, 0x00000007);
8179       andl(len, 0xFFFFFFF8);
8180       jccb(Assembler::zero, copy_tail);
8181 
8182       pmovzxbw(tmp1, Address(src, 0));
8183       movdqu(Address(dst, 0), tmp1);
8184       addptr(src, 8);
8185       addptr(dst, 2 * 8);
8186 
8187       jmp(copy_tail, true);
8188     }
8189 
8190     // inflate 8 chars per iter
8191     bind(copy_8_loop);
8192     pmovzxbw(tmp1, Address(src, len, Address::times_1));  // unpack to 8 words
8193     movdqu(Address(dst, len, Address::times_2), tmp1);
8194     addptr(len, 8);
8195     jcc(Assembler::notZero, copy_8_loop);
8196 
8197     bind(copy_tail);
8198     movl(len, tmp2);
8199 
8200     cmpl(len, 4);
8201     jccb(Assembler::less, copy_bytes);
8202 
8203     movdl(tmp1, Address(src, 0));  // load 4 byte chars
8204     pmovzxbw(tmp1, tmp1);
8205     movq(Address(dst, 0), tmp1);
8206     subptr(len, 4);
8207     addptr(src, 4);
8208     addptr(dst, 8);
8209 
8210     bind(copy_bytes);
8211   } else {
8212     bind(below_threshold);
8213   }
8214 
8215   testl(len, len);
8216   jccb(Assembler::zero, done);
8217   lea(src, Address(src, len, Address::times_1));
8218   lea(dst, Address(dst, len, Address::times_2));
8219   negptr(len);
8220 
8221   // inflate 1 char per iter
8222   bind(copy_chars_loop);
8223   load_unsigned_byte(tmp2, Address(src, len, Address::times_1));  // load byte char
8224   movw(Address(dst, len, Address::times_2), tmp2);  // inflate byte char to word
8225   increment(len);
8226   jcc(Assembler::notZero, copy_chars_loop);
8227 
8228   bind(done);
8229 }
8230 
8231 #ifdef _LP64
8232 void MacroAssembler::convert_f2i(Register dst, XMMRegister src) {
8233   Label done;
8234   cvttss2sil(dst, src);
8235   // Conversion instructions do not match JLS for overflow, underflow and NaN -> fixup in stub
8236   cmpl(dst, 0x80000000); // float_sign_flip
8237   jccb(Assembler::notEqual, done);
8238   subptr(rsp, 8);
8239   movflt(Address(rsp, 0), src);
8240   call(RuntimeAddress(CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address, StubRoutines::x86::f2i_fixup())));
8241   pop(dst);
8242   bind(done);
8243 }
8244 
8245 void MacroAssembler::convert_d2i(Register dst, XMMRegister src) {
8246   Label done;
8247   cvttsd2sil(dst, src);
8248   // Conversion instructions do not match JLS for overflow, underflow and NaN -> fixup in stub
8249   cmpl(dst, 0x80000000); // float_sign_flip
8250   jccb(Assembler::notEqual, done);
8251   subptr(rsp, 8);
8252   movdbl(Address(rsp, 0), src);
8253   call(RuntimeAddress(CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address, StubRoutines::x86::d2i_fixup())));
8254   pop(dst);
8255   bind(done);
8256 }
8257 
8258 void MacroAssembler::convert_f2l(Register dst, XMMRegister src) {
8259   Label done;
8260   cvttss2siq(dst, src);
8261   cmp64(dst, ExternalAddress((address) StubRoutines::x86::double_sign_flip()));
8262   jccb(Assembler::notEqual, done);
8263   subptr(rsp, 8);
8264   movflt(Address(rsp, 0), src);
8265   call(RuntimeAddress(CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address, StubRoutines::x86::f2l_fixup())));
8266   pop(dst);
8267   bind(done);
8268 }
8269 
8270 void MacroAssembler::convert_d2l(Register dst, XMMRegister src) {
8271   Label done;
8272   cvttsd2siq(dst, src);
8273   cmp64(dst, ExternalAddress((address) StubRoutines::x86::double_sign_flip()));
8274   jccb(Assembler::notEqual, done);
8275   subptr(rsp, 8);
8276   movdbl(Address(rsp, 0), src);
8277   call(RuntimeAddress(CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address, StubRoutines::x86::d2l_fixup())));
8278   pop(dst);
8279   bind(done);
8280 }
8281 
8282 void MacroAssembler::cache_wb(Address line)
8283 {
8284   // 64 bit cpus always support clflush
8285   assert(VM_Version::supports_clflush(), "clflush should be available");
8286   bool optimized = VM_Version::supports_clflushopt();
8287   bool no_evict = VM_Version::supports_clwb();
8288 
8289   // prefer clwb (writeback without evict) otherwise
8290   // prefer clflushopt (potentially parallel writeback with evict)
8291   // otherwise fallback on clflush (serial writeback with evict)
8292 
8293   if (optimized) {
8294     if (no_evict) {
8295       clwb(line);
8296     } else {
8297       clflushopt(line);
8298     }
8299   } else {
8300     // no need for fence when using CLFLUSH
8301     clflush(line);
8302   }
8303 }
8304 
8305 void MacroAssembler::cache_wbsync(bool is_pre)
8306 {
8307   assert(VM_Version::supports_clflush(), "clflush should be available");
8308   bool optimized = VM_Version::supports_clflushopt();
8309   bool no_evict = VM_Version::supports_clwb();
8310 
8311   // pick the correct implementation
8312 
8313   if (!is_pre && (optimized || no_evict)) {
8314     // need an sfence for post flush when using clflushopt or clwb
8315     // otherwise no no need for any synchroniaztion
8316 
8317     sfence();
8318   }
8319 }
8320 #endif // _LP64
8321 
8322 Assembler::Condition MacroAssembler::negate_condition(Assembler::Condition cond) {
8323   switch (cond) {
8324     // Note some conditions are synonyms for others
8325     case Assembler::zero:         return Assembler::notZero;
8326     case Assembler::notZero:      return Assembler::zero;
8327     case Assembler::less:         return Assembler::greaterEqual;
8328     case Assembler::lessEqual:    return Assembler::greater;
8329     case Assembler::greater:      return Assembler::lessEqual;
8330     case Assembler::greaterEqual: return Assembler::less;
8331     case Assembler::below:        return Assembler::aboveEqual;
8332     case Assembler::belowEqual:   return Assembler::above;
8333     case Assembler::above:        return Assembler::belowEqual;
8334     case Assembler::aboveEqual:   return Assembler::below;
8335     case Assembler::overflow:     return Assembler::noOverflow;
8336     case Assembler::noOverflow:   return Assembler::overflow;
8337     case Assembler::negative:     return Assembler::positive;
8338     case Assembler::positive:     return Assembler::negative;
8339     case Assembler::parity:       return Assembler::noParity;
8340     case Assembler::noParity:     return Assembler::parity;
8341   }
8342   ShouldNotReachHere(); return Assembler::overflow;
8343 }
8344 
8345 SkipIfEqual::SkipIfEqual(
8346     MacroAssembler* masm, const bool* flag_addr, bool value) {
8347   _masm = masm;
8348   _masm->cmp8(ExternalAddress((address)flag_addr), value);
8349   _masm->jcc(Assembler::equal, _label);
8350 }
8351 
8352 SkipIfEqual::~SkipIfEqual() {
8353   _masm->bind(_label);
8354 }
8355 
8356 // 32-bit Windows has its own fast-path implementation
8357 // of get_thread
8358 #if !defined(WIN32) || defined(_LP64)
8359 
8360 // This is simply a call to Thread::current()
8361 void MacroAssembler::get_thread(Register thread) {
8362   if (thread != rax) {
8363     push(rax);
8364   }
8365   LP64_ONLY(push(rdi);)
8366   LP64_ONLY(push(rsi);)
8367   push(rdx);
8368   push(rcx);
8369 #ifdef _LP64
8370   push(r8);
8371   push(r9);
8372   push(r10);
8373   push(r11);
8374 #endif
8375 
8376   MacroAssembler::call_VM_leaf_base(CAST_FROM_FN_PTR(address, Thread::current), 0);
8377 
8378 #ifdef _LP64
8379   pop(r11);
8380   pop(r10);
8381   pop(r9);
8382   pop(r8);
8383 #endif
8384   pop(rcx);
8385   pop(rdx);
8386   LP64_ONLY(pop(rsi);)
8387   LP64_ONLY(pop(rdi);)
8388   if (thread != rax) {
8389     mov(thread, rax);
8390     pop(rax);
8391   }
8392 }
8393 
8394 #endif // !WIN32 || _LP64
